Evelyn set her glass down with a sharp clink. She met his gaze with a cool smile. "No, thank you."

###Chapter 168

Lucas Laurier froze in place, his smile stiffening on his face.

"That can't be true. We just asked Ethan when you two were planning to have kids, and he said it was up to you..."

His sharp instincts told him Ethan hadn't informed their friend group about the divorce.

Evelyn Sullivan frowned slightly.

She didn’t understand why Ethan was keeping this a secret.

"We've already signed the divorce papers."

Lucas awkwardly rubbed his nose. The usually smooth-talking man found himself at a loss for words.

"Well... I should head back to the private room."

He practically fled the scene.

The private room door burst open.

"Ethan!" Lucas's voice rose sharply. "You and Evelyn are divorced, and you didn’t tell us?"

Ethan Sullivan and Ryan Paisley both looked up.

"Who told you that?" Ethan's gaze turned icy.

"I ran into Evelyn in the restroom. She said it herself." Lucas sighed. "From the moment Isabella returned, I knew this day would come..."

Ryan clenched his fists, his knuckles turning white.

So they were already divorced.

A secret flicker of joy stirred in his chest.

Ethan suddenly stood and strode out of the room.

In another corner of the restaurant, Evelyn was laughing with Zoe Zade.

A shadow fell over their table.

"Come with me." Ethan's voice was cold as ice.

Evelyn set down her chopsticks. "Whatever it is, can it wait—"

Before she could finish, his hand clamped around her wrist.

"Ethan, what are you doing?" Zoe slammed her hands on the table.

Evelyn shook her head at her, signaling her not to interfere.

Inside an empty private room, Ethan slammed the door shut.

"Why did you tell Lucas we're divorced?"

Evelyn met his gaze calmly. "Isn't it the truth?"

"Grandmother's health is fragile. She can't handle the shock."

"She agreed to the divorce when we signed the papers."

Ethan took a step closer. "She adores you. How could you bear to break her heart? Once you remarry, will you even visit her?"

Evelyn's lips curled into a cold smile. "So you expect me to keep up this charade for you?"

###Chapter 169

"I'll personally tell Grandma the truth within three months. Until then, I need you to keep this secret."

Evelyn frowned slightly, sensing something unspoken in Ethan's words.

"When exactly?"

"No later than three months."

Silence stretched between them before Evelyn reluctantly nodded.

"Fine. I hope you keep your word."

As she turned to leave, Ethan grabbed her wrist.

"You'll need to play along during this time. Every visit to Grandma requires your presence."

"Ethan!" She yanked her arm free. "Keeping this secret is already crossing my line!"

His gaze darkened. "Grandma's health has been declining since the last shock. I won't have her worrying about us."

"Understood." Her voice turned icy. "Anything else?"

He released her and shook his head.

"I'm leaving."

The private room door slammed shut. Ethan remained motionless, his fingertips still warm from her skin.

Returning to the VIP suite, Evelyn had lost her appetite. After picking at her food, she left the restaurant with Zoe.

"I must've been blind!" Zoe fumed in the car. "Arrogant control freaks are the worst!"

Evelyn changed the subject. "How did you meet Lucas Laurier?"

"That annoying investor!" Zoe rolled her eyes. "He keeps inviting me to dinner under the pretense of discussing Eternal Legacy, always so damn polite I can't even refuse properly!"

Lucas's flirtatious charm screamed playboy—exactly the type Zoe despised.

"Rumor says he changes girlfriends more often than shirts," Evelyn warned.

"Relax!" Zoe scoffed. "I hate players like him."

The memory of her mother excusing her father's endless betrayals haunted her. That childhood trauma had killed her belief in love.

"Just be careful."

"I'll quit acting once I save enough!" Zoe's eyes sparkled. "Open a little bookstore somewhere anonymous—just reading and sunbathing all day."

Back at Northville Villa, Evelyn buried herself in paperwork until late evening. Rubbing her stiff neck, she emerged from the study past ten.

Her phone buzzed with William's caller ID.

"Evelyn, where are you?"

Her tone chilled. "What do you want?"

After an endless pause, he finally spoke. "Come home. We need to talk."

###Chapter 170

Evelyn's cold voice came through the phone. "Get to the point."

William's tone was awkward. "The Sullivan Group is developing the Eastside Project... Could you put in a word for me?"

Evelyn let out a soft laugh. "Do you really think he'd listen to me?"

"You're his wife—"

"Sorry. Can't help."

The call ended abruptly.

William's face darkened instantly. He slammed his phone onto the couch.

Victoria sneered beside him. "I told you she's an ungrateful wretch!"

"We never should have brought her back," William growled through clenched teeth.

Isabella walked in to find her parents sitting stiffly in the living room, their expressions stormy.

"What's wrong?"

Victoria immediately launched into her complaint. "It's that precious sister of yours!"

After hearing the story, Isabella soothed them gently. "Let me try."

Back in her room, Isabella dialed Ethan's number.

The phone rang for a long time before he answered.

"What is it?"

His voice was icy.

Isabella softened her tone. "Ethan, about the Eastside Project—"

"Isabella." Ethan cut her off sharply. "This isn't a game."

The line went dead.

Isabella gripped her phone so tightly her nails dug into her palm.

Sullivan Group CEO Office.

Ethan stared at the documents on his desk before speaking abruptly. "Has William been here?"

Colin nodded. "Three times."

"Next time, tell him directly," Ethan said, his gaze frigid. "The Jackson Group isn't qualified."

###Chapter 171

"Mr. Sullivan, is there a problem?"

Ethan Sullivan remained silent for a long moment, his fingers tapping lightly on the desk.

"Look into that land project. See which smaller contracts can be allocated to the Jacksons."

Colin Keller's eyes flickered with surprise, but he quickly masked it.

"I'll get right on it."

The office fell back into silence. Ethan picked up his phone, staring at Evelyn Sullivan's profile picture on the screen. After a long pause, he locked the device.

Three hours later, Colin returned with documents.

"Mr. Sullivan, the swimming pool and landscaping contracts can be outsourced to the Jacksons."

"Contact William Jackson." Ethan paused. "Next time he comes, let him through without delay."

Colin nodded and left, his mind reeling.

The change was too sudden. Even during Ethan's passionate relationship with Isabella, he had never shown favoritism to the Jacksons. Unless... this was for Evelyn?

Colin suddenly understood. He'd have to treat William with more respect from now on—this was his future father-in-law.

At the Jackson villa, Isabella had just calmed down and was preparing for bed when her door was knocked open urgently.

"Isabella!" Victoria Farley beamed with excitement. "Did you contact Ethan?"

Isabella froze, remembering the rejected call earlier.

"Mom, actually—"

"Your father just got word! The Sullivans are giving the Eastside Project to our family!" Victoria clasped her daughter's hands. "I knew you could make it happen!"

Isabella's pupils contracted. Ethan had been so cold on the phone—how could this be?

"I... I'm just so happy," she forced a smile.

Victoria lovingly stroked her hair. "This project will bring in at least a hundred million. What reward would you like?"

"Nothing, Mom."

"That six-million-dollar dress—we'll go buy it tomorrow."

Isabella's eyes lit up as she threw herself into Victoria's arms. "Thank you, Mom!"

The next morning, Evelyn had just picked up her car keys when her phone rang.

"Evelyn!" Sophia Reynolds' voice was urgent. "Glorious is suing us for copyright infringement!"

###Chapter 172

Evelyn Sullivan frowned. "What happened?"

"MY's designs from last quarter just launched yesterday and sold out instantly. But this morning, a plagiarism scandal exploded. Glorious sent us a cease-and-desist letter!"

Sophia Reynolds trembled with anger. She had personally reviewed those designs—there was no way they were plagiarized.

"Send me the accused designs. Do we have photos of Glorious's piece?"

"No physical images, but Glorious claims they have stock at Qanda Mall. I was about to head there."

Evelyn checked her watch. "The mall isn't open yet. Let’s return to the office first. Bring the designer to my office."

"What about the online backlash?"

"Stay silent for now. We don’t want to give them ammunition."

Half an hour later, Yvonne Young, a timid new designer, stood nervously before Evelyn’s desk. No one would expect such bold designs from this shy girl.

Sophia handed her a glass of water. "Relax. Tell us when you designed this piece. Do you still have the original draft?"

"It was completed on May 3rd and uploaded to the cloud that same day." Yvonne’s eyes reddened. "Sophia, I swear I didn’t copy anything!"

"I believe you." Sophia reassured her. "Walk us through your inspiration and design process."

By the time the sun dipped low, Sophia had compiled all the timelines. Evelyn closed the folder. "Time to face Glorious."

The online images only showed a vague resemblance, but they needed to examine the details in person.

Qanda Mall blazed with lights. The moment they approached Glorious’s entrance, a clerk blocked them.

"Sorry. MY employees aren’t allowed inside."

Sophia smirked. "What’s wrong? Afraid we’ll expose you?"

The clerk forced a smile. "Only plagiarists would say that."

"You—"

Evelyn yanked Sophia back before she could lunge. Dragging her away, Evelyn’s eyes darkened.

"They were prepared for us. The cease-and-desist is just the beginning. This might end up in court."

Sophia kicked a pebble in frustration. "Cowards!"

"Back to the office." Evelyn glanced at the mall’s security cameras. "I’ll find a way to get that dress."

###Chapter 173

Sophia slammed her palm against the bathroom sink, sending icy droplets splashing onto her face.

"I can't swallow this insult!"

She whirled around and stormed out of the restroom, her stilettos clicking sharply against the marble floor.

Evelyn Sullivan leaned against the railing, her fingers gliding swiftly across her phone screen. The moment she sent Vanessa Cruz's message, she locked her phone and lifted her gaze to the massive advertisement hanging in the mall atrium.

The plagiarism scandal loomed like a ticking time bomb, threatening to obliterate MY Fashion Group at any moment.

"Evelyn Sullivan!"

A shrill voice sliced through the air.

Evelyn turned slowly to see Victoria Farley striding toward her, Isabella Jackson clinging to her arm. The luxury shopping bag in Isabella's hand gleamed under the lights, its prominent logo impossible to miss.

Victoria closed the distance in quick strides, her meticulously groomed brows furrowed in anger.

"Too busy to see us yesterday, but now you have time to shop?"

Evelyn's lips curled into a cold smile.

"Mrs. Farley, you never even fulfilled your duty as a mother. What right do you have to demand anything from me?"

Victoria's crimson-nailed fingers clenched into fists.

"We took you back into the Jackson family at sixteen. Did we ever deprive you of food or clothes? Did you lack anything Isabella had?"

Evelyn studied Victoria's twisted expression and found it almost laughable.

"Are you done?"

She turned to leave, but Victoria seized her wrist.

"When are you filing for divorce?"

Evelyn's gaze flicked to Isabella's suddenly pale face. A soft chuckle escaped her.

"In such a hurry to take my place?"

Isabella's lips trembled.

"Ethan doesn't love you..."

"Did he tell you that himself?"

"Everyone can see it!"

Evelyn nodded, her eyes filled with pity.

"So not only are you a scheming little snake, but you're also blind."

Victoria's shriek drew stares from passersby.

"Divorce him now, or you'll regret it!"

Evelyn leisurely extracted her wrist from Victoria's grip.

"Who was it that publicly disowned me at the press conference? What gives you the right to order me around now?"

Victoria shook with rage.

"Pay back every cent the Jacksons spent on you!"

Evelyn's expression turned glacial.

"Fine. Let Isabella vomit up my bone marrow first."

Victoria staggered back a step, and Isabella hurried to steady her.

"Mom, she's just confused right now..."

"She's an ungrateful wretch!" Victoria spat through gritted teeth. Then she turned to Isabella. "Your father wants to invite Ethan to dinner. You'll go personally."

Isabella nodded obediently, a glimmer of triumph flashing in her eyes.

###Chapter 174

Isabella's fingers trembled slightly as she whispered, "Okay."

On the way home with Victoria, her mind wandered. Only when she stood at the foot of the Sullivan Group building did she take a deep breath, steady herself, and step into the elevator.

"Ethan." She forced a sweet smile, but it froze when she met his icy gaze.

"What do you want?"

"Dad would like to invite you to dinner to thank you for including Jackson Corp in the Eastside Project." She hesitated, then added, "Just our family."

Ethan didn’t look up from his files. "Will Evelyn be there?"

Isabella's smile shattered. Her grip tightened on her purse strap, nails digging into her palms.

"You... want her to come?"

"She's my wife." His sharp gaze finally lifted, cutting through her like a blade. "Shouldn't your father invite her too?"

Tears burned behind her eyes. "I'll ask Dad to let her know."

Outside, the sunlight stung. She wanted to storm back in and scream at him—why give her hope just to crush it?

But she didn’t dare.

At home, Victoria rushed to meet her. "Well? Did he agree?"

"Yes." Isabella bit her lip. "But... Ethan wants Evelyn there."

Victoria's face darkened. "Why would we invite her?"

"Mom..." Her voice wavered. "Maybe we should call her?"

"Absolutely not!" Victoria snapped. "That ungrateful girl doesn’t care about this family!"

William sat silently on the couch.

Isabella picked up her phone and dialed the long-unused number. It rang endlessly before connecting.

"What do you want?" Evelyn's voice was glacial.

Isabella relayed the invitation. A cold laugh echoed through the line.

"Not interested."

"But—"

The call ended abruptly. Tears spilled down Isabella's cheeks.

"She... hung up on me."

Victoria pulled her into a hug. "Forget her! Good riddance!"

Meanwhile, in the MY Fashion Group office...

Evelyn had just set down her phone when Vanessa called.

"Boss, I got the dresses."

"Leave them at reception."

She rubbed her temples. Ten minutes later, Bianca delivered the package.

Evelyn unwrapped it, spreading both garments on her desk. Her fingers traced the fabric, her expression hardening with every inch.

"Sophia, come here."

When Sophia saw the nearly identical designs, she trembled with rage.

"Glorious has no shame! This is blatant plagiarism!"

Evelyn shook her head. "They released theirs two months before us."

"But Yvonne has the original sketches—"

"If Glorious wasn’t confident, they wouldn’t publicly accuse us." Evelyn’s voice was eerily calm. "Until we have proof, we don’t take sides."

Sophia gnawed her lip. "So we just let this go?"

Evelyn stared out the window, her eyes shadowed.

"Of course not."

###Chapter 175

"Yvonne's designs are completely original! I watched her revise them three times myself!" Sophia Reynolds slammed her palm on the table in agitation.

Evelyn Sullivan massaged her temples and turned the laptop screen toward her. "See for yourself. The similarity exceeds 90%."

Sophia stared at the screen, her fingers tightening unconsciously.

"I refuse to believe she'd plagiarize..."

"If it's not plagiarism, then it's a leak." Evelyn shut the laptop. "Glorious started small-scale production of this design three months ago, waiting for today."

Sophia's face turned ashen, her lips trembling slightly.

"I'm going to confront her right now!"

"Stop." Evelyn's voice turned icy. "Alerting them now will only make things worse."

——

At the penthouse of Brocade Tower, Jason Zade swirled his wine glass with a satisfied smile. "Director Young, this move was brilliant."

Mason Young took a sip, his eyes glinting shrewdly. "The shares you promised me, Mr. Zade..."

"Don't worry. The contract will be in your hands the day MY Fashion Group goes under."

An assistant hurried in. "Director Young, the trending topic is live."

Mason nodded approvingly. "Keep pushing. I want MY to have no chance of recovery."

——

Evelyn's fingers flew across the keyboard.

The screen displayed: Mason Young, Creative Director of Glorious, Yvonne Young's uncle.

A cold smirk curved her lips as she dialed a private investigator. "Dig deeper. I want records of all their financial transactions."

——

As dusk fell, Evelyn approached her doorstep to the sound of a heated argument.

"Mr. Laurier, I said no means no!" Zoe Zade's cheeks flushed crimson with anger.

Lucas Laurier leaned against his sports car, grinning lazily. "I'll double the penalty fee."

Zoe immediately linked arms with her. "Evelyn, this guy won't take no for an answer about some ad..."

Zoe rolled her eyes and tugged Evelyn inside. "Not worth my time!"

Lucas called after them, "I'll be back tomorrow."

Evelyn gazed thoughtfully at the darkening sky outside.

###Chapter 176

"You haven't even heard what I need help with yet, sis-in-law."

Evelyn Sullivan pressed her lips together, her expression distant. "Mr. Laurier, I don't think there's anything left between us that requires assistance."

After the divorce, she had no intention of staying entangled with Ethan Sullivan's circle.

The moment they stepped into the villa, Zoe Zade rolled her eyes.

"That Lucas Laurier is like a persistent ghost! He ambushed me three times today, insisting I endorse his new product. If not for his status, I would've called the police!"

Evelyn couldn't help but laugh.

Lucas was notorious in high society for being a heartthrob. If he knew how much Zoe despised him, he'd probably choke on his own pride.

"The endorsement fee must be decent. Consider it a side gig."

Zoe gave her a strange look. "Do you know what he's selling?"

"Hmm?"

"Condoms."

Evelyn nearly choked on her water. "Is he insane?"

"If I weren't worried about future retaliation, I'd suggest he check himself into a psychiatric ward."

Dinner was prepared by Zoe, who had inherited her mother's culinary skills. In comparison, Evelyn's cooking was barely edible.

After the meal, Evelyn sprawled on the couch, too lazy to move.

Zoe tugged at her. "Don't lie down right after eating. Let's take a walk."

The night was pleasant. By the time they returned from their stroll through the villa grounds, Lucas' car was gone.

As Evelyn settled in to check her emails after her shower, her phone buzzed.

[Picking you up tomorrow morning.]

She frowned. There shouldn't be any reason for her and Ethan to meet anytime soon. She chose to ignore it.

In VIP Room 8888, the clatter of mahjong tiles filled the air.

Ethan and Lucas were visibly distracted.

"I'm done." Ryan Paisley pushed the tiles away. "What's wrong with you two tonight?"

Ethan picked up his phone and stood. "Going for a smoke."

Ryan smirked. "Waiting for Isabella's reply?"

"No."

At the end of the hallway, Ethan stared at the unanswered message on his screen, an inexplicable tightness in his chest.

It suddenly struck him how empty the villa had felt since she moved out.

"Something wrong?"

The familiar voice on the other end made him realize he'd dialed her number.

"You saw my message?"

"I did."

"Why didn't you reply?"

"I thought you sent it to the wrong person."

###Chapter 177

Evelyn Sullivan stared at her phone screen, fingers hovering over the keyboard. She deleted the drafted message and typed again: "Work has been hectic lately. I'll visit Grandma another day."

Ethan Sullivan's reply popped up instantly: "Who said anything about visiting Grandma?"

She frowned, fingers flying across the screen: "Then why are you contacting me?"

"Didn't Isabella tell you?" His message carried obvious irritation.

"Evelyn Sullivan, what's your last name?" His voice was icy.

"Mr. Sullivan, I'm busy—"

"Six p.m. tomorrow. I'll pick you up at the office." He cut her off decisively before hanging up.

The next morning at MY Fashion Group.

Sophia Reynolds entered the CEO's office to find Evelyn standing by the floor-to-ceiling window. Sunlight gilded her silhouette but couldn't dispel the chill surrounding her.

Evelyn walked to the window. Camera crews clustered at the entrance, flashes popping like fireworks.

"Call security." Her gaze drifted to a distant black sedan where a shadowy figure watched through binoculars.

###Chapter 178

Quincy froze, clearly unprepared for Evelyn's unyielding stance.

"I'll handle it right away."

"Wait."

"If the police prove useless, hire a team of bodyguards instead."

Anna?

The elusive founder of MY?

"Bring her here."

Colin hurried after Evelyn just as she was about to enter the taxi.

"Ms. Sullivan, Mr. Sullivan is waiting for you."

"Tell him I don't have time for dinner."

"If you refuse, I'll be in trouble."

Evelyn chuckled.

"Relax. He'd replace his wife before he replaces his secretary."

"Back to the office."

Ethan's voice was icy.

In the private dining room of the Jackson residence, Isabella swayed gracefully in a lavender chiffon gown, the cinched waist accentuating her slender figure.

The skirt fluttered with her movements like a budding water lily.

Victoria surveyed her daughter with satisfaction.

This was the refined heiress she had meticulously raised—every gesture exuded elegance.

###Chapter 179

Evelyn Sullivan had only spent a few years with the Jackson family, barely shedding her provincial air. Every time Victoria Farley thought of her adopted daughter, disgust welled up in her heart.

If Evelyn had obediently served the family’s interests, Victoria might have spared her a few kind words. Now? She wished Evelyn would disappear forever.

William Jackson checked his watch for the third time, his frown deepening. Ethan Sullivan was half an hour late with no sign of arrival.

"Isabella, call Mr. Sullivan," William said impatiently.

Isabella Jackson dialed three times, her expression darkening. "Dad, Ethan isn’t answering..."

William immediately called Colin Keller. When the call ended, his face was stormy.

On the other end, Evelyn coldly hung up. Subsequent calls went unanswered.

"Find her! Track her down now!" William barked at his secretary.

At the villa, Evelyn had just finished dinner with Zoe Zade when the doorbell rang abruptly.

Victoria cut in shrilly, "If it’s shares you’re after, using such despicable methods only makes us loathe you more!"

Evelyn studied them as if they were strangers. "Isn’t Isabella so capable? Let her beg Ethan again."

"Why should Isabella clean up your mess?" Victoria snapped. "Apologize to Mr. Sullivan immediately!"

Evelyn suddenly smiled.

"What are you laughing at?!"

"At how ridiculous you are." Her voice was calm. "I’ve done nothing wrong. Why should I apologize?"

Victoria raised her hand to strike, but a slender hand caught her wrist.

Zoe shoved Victoria back. "What kind of rabid dog barks at someone’s doorstep?"

Victoria staggered, shaking with rage. "Evelyn! What lowlife friends have you brought into this house?"

"Shut up!" Evelyn’s gaze sharpened like a blade. "You have no right to judge my friends."

###Chapter 180

Victoria Farley's chest heaved with rage, her nails digging deep into her palms.

"Look at what you've become! Corrupted by these lowlifes!"

Evelyn Sullivan leaned against the doorframe, her gaze icy.

"What I become is none of your concern."

The moment the call connected, his deep voice came through. "Evelyn?"

Three seconds of silence.

"Where are you? I'll come now."

Evelyn scoffed and slammed the door shut.

The loud bang made Victoria stagger back, nearly falling.

"You ungrateful brat!" Victoria shrieked, pounding on the door.

When had she become this shrill, calculating shrew?

Perhaps when he first glimpsed the scheming beneath her sweet facade.

"Ethan!"

"Evelyn, open the door."

###Chapter 181

###Chapter 182

"Mom, it's not what you think..."

Victoria Farley shook off Isabella Jackson's reaching hand and slipped into the car without looking back.

It hit her then—the man she'd shared a bed with for two decades was no longer the doting husband from years ago.

When the Mercedes stopped at the Jackson estate, Victoria stumbled out. She missed the disgust flashing in William's eyes—like she was outdated furniture.

Isabella returned to find her mother weeping alone.

"Mom, it's all my fault..." She threw herself at Victoria's knees. "I thought Ethan only..."

Isabella nestled into her mother's arms, the ghost of a smirk playing on her lips.

###Chapter 183

Victoria's nails dug deep into her palms as tears welled in her eyes. "Isabella, your father said...he'll divorce me if I don't apologize to Evelyn."

Isabella's pupils constricted violently. The teacup in her hand nearly slipped. "What?!"

"Don't worry, Mom." Isabella grasped her mother's trembling hands, shadows flickering in her eyes. "I'll handle this."

Back in her room, Isabella swept all the bottles and jars off her vanity. The realization that Ethan would reject her pleas yet make exceptions for Evelyn cut like a knife.

She stared at her phone screen, lips curling into a cold smile.

"Ethan, remember those three wishes you owe me?"

"For my first wish..." Her crimson lips parted, each word dripping venom. "I want you to break up with Evelyn immediately."

Ethan's breath hitched audibly.

"Fine." The single word sounded wrenched from between gritted teeth.

Hanging up, Isabella studied her twisted reflection in the mirror. This game was hers to win.

......

Dawn light filtered through the curtains as Evelyn's phone screen illuminated.

She opened the file sent by the black-profile contact, fingers flying across the screen. A cold laugh escaped her when "Brocade" appeared in the text.

The ping of a bank transfer coincided with Zoe's voice calling from downstairs. "Evelyn, come quick!"

Tucking away her phone, Evelyn padded barefoot across the cold floorboards. Outside the window, an unexpected figure stood in the courtyard.

###Chapter 184

"Evelyn, look!" Sophia Reynolds yanked open the curtains and pointed toward the villa's entrance. "Isn't that Ethan Sullivan's secretary?"

Evelyn Sullivan walked to the window. In the morning light, Colin Keller stood out clearly, pacing back and forth with an exquisite food box in hand.

"He's been there for almost two hours," Sophia whispered. "Should we call the police?"

Evelyn smirked and headed downstairs. When she pushed open the front door, Colin immediately approached her.

"Miss Sullivan, Mr. Sullivan sent this especially for you." He handed her the box, its surface embossed with the gilded logo of "Rong's Kitchen."

Evelyn stared at the familiar emblem. Three years ago, she had waited in line for three hours just to buy their crab roe buns.

"Take it back," she said coldly. "Tell Ethan to stop wasting his time on meaningless gestures."

Colin hesitated. "But—"

"What?" Evelyn arched a brow. "Do I need to go to Sullivan Group myself?"

Before Colin could respond, a white BMW screeched to a halt by the curb. The door swung open, and Victoria Farley stormed over in her stilettos.

"Evelyn!" She grabbed Evelyn's wrist. "I came to apologize!"

Evelyn shook her off, her gaze flickering to Isabella Jackson hiding by the car. What game were these two playing now?

"Mrs. Farley, we have no ties left," she said, turning to leave.

Victoria blocked her path. "How can you be so heartless? I'm your mother!"

Evelyn laughed. "Wasn't it you who publicly disowned me at that press conference?"

Victoria's face turned ashen. Isabella rushed forward, linking arms with her. "Sis, Mom really means it this time..."

"Save it." Evelyn pulled open her car door and addressed Colin. "I'll be at Sullivan Group by noon."

The engine roared to life, drowning out Victoria's curses. Colin stood awkwardly as Isabella gave him a pitiful look.

"Colin, about Ethan—"

"Miss Jackson," he took a step back, "I'm not at liberty to discuss the CEO's affairs."

Back in the car, Victoria trembled with rage.

"That ungrateful wretch!" She slammed her fist against the seat. "I should've—"

"Mom!" Isabella cut her off. "What's the point of saying that now?"

Victoria suddenly seized her daughter's hand. "Isabella, Ethan clearly likes you. Why is he helping that bitch?"

Isabella turned away, her nails digging into her palms.

The midday sun scorched the Sullivan Group building. Evelyn stood in the elevator, watching the numbers climb. It was time to end this farce.

###Chapter 185

Evelyn Sullivan stepped through the revolving doors of Sullivan Tower, her heels clicking against the marble floor.

The receptionist blocked her path.

"Miss Sullivan, Mr. Sullivan has given strict orders not to receive any visitors today."

Evelyn narrowed her eyes, fingers flying across her phone screen. Five unanswered calls to Ethan Sullivan.

A cold smile curved her lips as she dialed Colin Keller instead.

Still no answer.

Her grip tightened around the burning phone as she typed a message: "How impressive, Mr. Sullivan. Cutting me off completely now?"

She turned to leave—only to collide with Ryan Paisley in his tailored suit.

"Miss Sullivan?" Surprise flickered in his eyes. "Here to see Ethan?"

Her expression instantly brightened, a sly tilt to her gaze. "Perfect timing, Ryan. Mind taking me upstairs?"

His Adam's apple bobbed. "You two..."

Ryan's eyes darkened. Reason screamed at him to refuse, but that hopeful look undid him. "Fine."

When the receptionist protested, Ryan silenced her with a glance. "She's with me. Any issues, take it up with me."

The elevator ascended to the penthouse.

The office door swung open—Ethan's pen snapped in half.

"Ryan. Out."

Ryan shielded Evelyn. "I insisted on bringing her—"

"Get out!"

Evelyn gently tugged Ryan's sleeve. "You should go."

The moment the door closed, her smile vanished. She strode to Ethan's desk and sat.

She met his icy stare. "When you refuse to see me, I find other ways."

"Stay away from him." He seized her wrist. "Or else—"

"Or else what?" She wrenched free, eyes blazing. "Ethan Sullivan, who gave you the right to control me?"

###Chapter 186

Evelyn Sullivan was utterly baffled. When had she ever provoked Ryan Paisley? She'd merely run into him by chance and asked for directions.

"I came here today to tell you—stop bothering me!" Her voice was icy.

"Are you hungry?"

Ethan Sullivan abruptly changed the subject. Evelyn frowned. "Are you even listening to me?"

"Let's eat first. I haven't had lunch yet."

She took a deep breath, forcing down her anger. "Ethan Sullivan, we're over!"

"Impossible." He set down the documents in his hand and met her gaze. "I don't agree."

Dark currents swirled in his deep eyes. Evelyn instinctively took half a step back.

"Since when do you get a say? You signed the divorce papers faster than anyone!"

"Because..." He stood and closed the distance between them. "I'm courting you again."

Evelyn let out a disbelieving laugh. "Since when did Mr. Sullivan learn to joke?"

"I'm serious."

"Enough!"

She turned to leave, but a strong hand yanked her back.

"Let go!"

Ethan effortlessly pinned her to the sofa. "You're not leaving until after lunch."

"Looking at you makes me sick!"

"What a coincidence." His low chuckle sent shivers down her spine. "Looking at you gives me an appetite."

Evelyn trembled with rage. This bastard!

"Eat or not?" He leisurely undid his cufflinks. "If you refuse, you'll stay here and keep me company while I work."

Knowing he meant it, she gritted her teeth and picked up the bowl. She finished the meal in three bites.

"Can I leave now?"

Ethan glanced at the half-eaten rice still in her bowl and arched a brow. "I'm not done yet."

Her nails dug into her palms. Out of the corner of her eye, she watched him calmly eating from the dishes she'd touched. A sharp pang shot through her chest.

In the past, he'd sanitized serving chopsticks three times before using them.

###Chapter 187

Evelyn Sullivan had always assumed Ethan Sullivan suffered from severe mysophobia.

That was until the family dinner where she witnessed Old Mrs. Sullivan feeding him with chopsticks still glistening with her saliva.

He ate without flinching.

Meanwhile, the shrimp she'd meticulously picked for him grew cold in his bowl before being dumped into the trash.

Twenty minutes passed before Ethan finished dabbing his mouth with a napkin.

"Can you let go now?" Evelyn shook her numb wrist.

This time, he released her without hesitation.

As the elevator doors closed, she exhaled in relief. She needed to shake off this persistent man—fast.

"Are you alright, Evelyn?" Ryan Paisley approached, his suit sleeves stained with fresh coffee.

Warmth flickered in her chest. "I owe you a dry-cleaning bill. Let me treat you to dinner sometime."

"Then I'm picking the most expensive restaurant." He flashed a grin, his canine teeth peeking through.

Among Ethan's inner circle, Ryan was the only one who never looked down on her. The others maintained polite facades while secretly blaming her for breaking up their golden couple.

"Ryan." Ethan's voice cut through the air like ice. "Finished reviewing the contract?"

The hallway temperature plummeted.

Without turning, Evelyn strode toward the elevator. "Don't let me keep you, Ryan. We'll talk later."

The polished doors reflected Ethan's stormy expression. His knuckles whitened as he watched her retreating figure.

"You two seem close." Ethan's gaze frosted over when he turned.

Ryan straightened his files. "We exchanged pleasantries during my hospital visits."

"Stay away from her."

"You're dating?!" Sophia Reynolds sprayed奶茶 across her spreadsheets.

###Chapter 188

Seeing Evelyn's confidence, Sophia's tense shoulders finally relaxed. "Fine. I'll get it done."

The resignation process went suspiciously smoothly. Standing outside the MY building with a cardboard box in her arms, Yvonne felt something was off. But the thought of her new position as chief designer at Brocade quickly pushed her doubts aside.

"Uncle, I quit!" That night, Yvonne excitedly called Mason Young.

His voice was low on the other end. "Report to Brocade tomorrow. Remember—use your new pen name."

After hanging up, Yvonne rolled around on her bed in excitement. She didn’t notice the flash of a camera shutter outside her window.

Meanwhile, the glow of Evelyn’s computer screen cast an eerie blue light. Her fingers brushed over a design file, pausing at the signature—Bianca Quinn.

The next morning, Evelyn stood before a rundown apartment building. The peeling paint on the door of Unit 301 barely held the numbers in place.

The girl who answered eyed her warily. "Who are you?"

"Someone who can help you reclaim what’s yours." Evelyn pulled a design sketch from her bag. "This 'Starlight' series—the real creator is you, isn’t it?"

Bianca’s pupils contracted. Her fingers whitened around the doorknob.

Two hours later, an explosive headline dominated the trending list: #Glorious Fashion Accused of Plagiarism#. The accompanying image showed two nearly identical design drafts, dated six months apart.

Public opinion flipped overnight. Glorious, once hailed as an originality pioneer, became the target of widespread condemnation. Even more shocking—netizens uncovered the true identity of Glorious’ new designer: Yvonne Young, the very person embroiled in MY’s plagiarism scandal.

Inside Brocade’s headquarters, Yvonne stared at her computer screen, sweat soaking through her shirt. Her trembling fingers dialed Mason’s number, only to be met with a cold dial tone.

Evelyn stood by the floor-to-ceiling windows of MY’s executive office when her phone lit up with a message from Sophia: "Glorious just released a statement."

###Chapter 189

The official statement from Glorious sent the comment section into chaos.

"LOL, this press release sounds so convincing."

"Waiting for the truth to come out."

The irony? When Glorious had accused MY of plagiarism, their "evidence" only predated MY's design by a week.

Public opinion flipped instantly.

"Joke of the year: The plagiarist cries plagiarism."

SLAP!

###Chapter 190

Bianca rose to her feet, her black trench coat sweeping behind her in a sharp arc.

Bianca wrenched her hand free, her gaze icy.

"Don't bother. We've already transferred hospitals."

In the VIP ward of First Hospital, Bianca's mother, Mrs. Quinn, was frantically packing her belongings.

"Mom!" Bianca rushed to stop her. "What are you doing?"

"Do you know how much this room costs per day?" Mrs. Quinn fretted, wringing her hands. "I can stay in a regular ward. Go cancel this right now!"

"No caregiver!" Mrs. Quinn waved her hands dismissively. "I'm feeling much better now. I can—"

A violent coughing fit cut her off. Bianca steadied her frail shoulders, realizing just how thin her mother had become beneath the hospital gown—her bones protruding sharply.

"The caregiver is non-negotiable." Bianca's voice tightened. "If you don't cooperate with treatment, I'll quit my job and stay by your side every day."

Mrs. Quinn finally relented with a sigh. As she stroked her daughter's soft hair, she noticed new black strands growing at the tips.

"Bianca... did you dye your hair?"

Bianca hesitated before forcing a smile. "Yes. Just wanted a change."

She didn't tell her mother that those were white hairs from three sleepless months of designing for others. But now, those days of toiling in the shadows were finally over.

Outside the window, magnolia buds peeked through the branches. Bianca tightened her grip on the employee badge in her pocket—finally bearing her own name.

###Chapter 191

"Evelyn! The internet is on fire!"

Cheers filled the room.

"Boss, you're the best!"

"Check Ins! That whistleblower just posted again!"

Every face paled.

###Chapter 192

88th floor, Sullivan Group headquarters.

###Chapter 193: Bloodstained Dusk

The setting sun stretched Ethan Sullivan's shadow long across the plaza before the Sullivan Group headquarters. ###Chapter 194

Slap!

###Chapter 196

###Chapter 197

Scorpion.
