"Isabella jumped because Ethan Sullivan gave her a taste of her own medicine after she drugged me. She had no way out."

Victoria grabbed her wrist. "You just stood by and let Ethan do that to your own sister?!"

Evelyn shook her off. "I used to think you were just biased. Now I see you have no sense of right and wrong."

"Evelyn Sullivan!"

"I've repaid any debt I owed you long ago." Evelyn enunciated each word clearly. "Tell Isabella that if she dares cause more trouble, I'll leave her with nothing."

Victoria froze in place as Evelyn turned and stepped into the elevator.

Inside the hospital room, Sophia Reynolds looked at her uncle with disappointment. "Uncle Simon, the company's annual dividends are substantial. Why would you do this?"

Simon's face darkened. "Whose side are you on? I'm your own uncle!"

"I stand with the truth, not family ties." Sophia gave a bitter smile. "Did you think about us being family when you took those kickbacks?"

"How dare you accuse me!" Simon slammed his hand against the bed. "Show me the evidence if you have any!"

"If you admit it now, there might still be time—"

"Get out!"

Evelyn had just exited the hospital when her phone rang.

###Chapter 239

"Ms. Sullivan, we have a buyer willing to purchase your villa in full. The contract is ready. Are you available to come sign it now?"

Evelyn Sullivan paused while organizing her files, surprise flickering in her eyes.

"That fast?"

"Yes. The buyer didn’t even negotiate the price—just paid the deposit immediately."

After hanging up, she texted Sophia Reynolds and hurriedly hailed a cab to Grand View Villas.

The agent called three more times during the ride, growing increasingly excited with each call.

"Ms. Sullivan, this buyer is incredibly decisive. They didn’t even check the property deed before agreeing to sign!"

A faint unease settled in Evelyn’s chest.

When she pushed open the villa’s front door and saw the tall figure standing by the floor-to-ceiling windows, realization struck.

"Ethan?"

The man turned. His suit was immaculate, his tie perfectly knotted beneath his Adam’s apple.

"Long time no see."

The agent rubbed his hands together. "Oh, you two know each other? Then the contract—"

"Deal’s off."

Evelyn spun on her heel and walked out, her heels clicking sharply against the marble floor.

Ethan caught up in a few strides, gripping her wrist.

"Reason?"

"You know why." She yanked her hand free. "You gave me this place in the divorce. Now you want to buy it back? Playing games with me?"

He suddenly leaned in, his warm breath brushing her ear.

"Remember what you said by the pool that night?"

Her ears burned.

"Disgusting!"

"I’m just stating facts." He straightened, his gaze unwavering. "You’ll come back eventually."

"In your dreams!" Her chest heaved with anger. "I’ll list it with another agency tomorrow!"

Ethan adjusted his cuffs leisurely. "Go ahead and try."

Three days later, she finally understood his meaning—every agency she contacted turned her down the next day.

A ringing phone interrupted her thoughts.

"Ms. Elia, we’d like to invite you to the design competition’s award ceremony—"

"Not interested."

Hanging up, she massaged her temples and pushed open Sophia’s office door.

"Hot pot?"

Sophia looked up from her paperwork. "Perfect timing. These reports are driving me insane."

They chose a trendy new hot pot restaurant. The moment they stepped inside, they ran into Alexander King and Lucas Laurier exiting a private room.

Sophia immediately turned to leave, but Alexander had already spotted them.

###Chapter 240 

"What a coincidence, sis-in-law!" Alexander King's voice rang out behind her.

Evelyn Sullivan paused mid-step but continued walking without turning around.

Sophia Reynolds whirled around with a cold smirk. "Move aside, Mr. King. You're blocking our way."

Alexander's smile froze, pain flickering in his eyes.

Lucas Laurier stifled a laugh and muttered under his breath, "Serves you right for trampling on her feelings."

"Shut up," Alexander growled through clenched teeth. "That actress you're chasing hasn't given you the time of day either."

"Not the same." Lucas waved his phone triumphantly. "At least she texts me back."

Alexander rolled his eyes, but before he could retort, Lucas had already dialed Ethan Sullivan's number.

"Guess who we ran into at the hot pot place?"

A beat of silence.

"Evelyn's here," Lucas drawled deliberately. "Looks upset. Ordering drinks..."

"Send me the address."

Hanging up, Lucas shot Alexander a smug look. "Take notes."

Meanwhile, Sophia had poured them both generous glasses.

"Drink up, Evelyn." Her eyes were red-rimmed. "To surviving the storm. And to finally seeing certain people for who they really are."

Evelyn silently raised her glass, watching Sophia's trembling fingers.

Two drinks in, Sophia's words began slurring as she listed Alexander's countless faults. Evelyn rested her chin on her palm, the world around her blurring.

When Ethan arrived, he found two women slumped drunkenly over the table.

"What happened?" His brow furrowed.

Lucas shrugged. "Who knew they'd be such lightweights?"

Ethan strode forward and scooped Evelyn into his arms. She squirmed, pressing her flushed cheek against his cool suit jacket with a contented sigh.

"Stay still," he warned lowly.

Evelyn blinked up at him through hazy eyes, then suddenly poked his sharp jawline. "You're... really pretty..."

Ethan froze, his gaze darkening.

"See Sophia home," he ordered without looking back, carrying Evelyn away.

In the car, intoxicated fingers fumbled with buttons. Ethan caught her wrist, voice rough. "Behave."

"Hot..." she whined, eyes glistening.

His Adam's apple bobbed as he slammed the partition button. "Drive faster."

Cool autumn air slipped through the cracked window. Curled against him, Evelyn murmured unconsciously, "Ethan..."

His arms tightened around her.

###Chapter 241

Evelyn blinked her bleary eyes and shook her head in confusion. "No, my home is in Elm Cove. I need to go back."

"That's Daniel Sterling's house!" Ethan's voice turned icy. "It has nothing to do with you!"

Had he not confirmed Daniel was away filming, he would never have allowed her to stay there.

"Nonsense!" Her voice cracked with sudden emotion, eyes reddening. "That is my home! That cold mausoleum called Grand View isn't home!"

Ethan had never seen her this vulnerable. His tone softened involuntarily. "Why would you say that? You lived at Grand View for three years."

"Three years means nothing!" A sob escaped her throat. "Thirty years wouldn't make it home! Besides... Ethan Sullivan and I are divorced!"

"Divorced?" His pupils constricted. "Not in this lifetime!"

Slap!

Evelyn's palm connected sharply with his cheek.

"Disgusting mosquito! Your buzzing hurts my ears! Stay away!"

Ethan's face darkened.

She scooted toward the car door, squinting at him. "Though this mosquito is quite handsome... just too fierce-looking."

"Evelyn Sullivan!"

Her eyes widened in terror. "The mosquito can talk?! It knows my name!" She flailed her arms wildly. "Back off! I'm a black belt! Hah!"

Regret twisted Ethan's gut. He should've let Lucas take her home.

Thud!

Her head hit the window with a dull crack.

"Oww..."

Ethan yanked her into his arms, massaging the injured spot with surprising gentleness. After feeble resistance, she went limp.

The nightmare came swiftly—a giant mosquito chasing her relentlessly until it morphed into Ethan's face, whispering horrifically: "I'll make you bear a swarm of baby mosquitoes!"

"Ahh!"

Evelyn jolted awake in Grand View's master bedroom. Her last memory was sharing hotpot with Sophia before two drinks erased everything.

Running water sounded from the bathroom. As she moved to rise, a shocking realization struck—she was completely naked. Clothing littered the floor, including her lace bra and a pair of black men's briefs.

Her breath hitched. Had she...?

The bathroom door swung open. She turned away hastily, feigning composure. "You should leave. I need rest. We'll... talk another time."

Ethan froze mid-towel-dry, eyes turning glacial. "Evelyn Sullivan. Repeat that."

###Chapter 242

Ethan Sullivan's voice was laced with frost, each syllable carrying a biting chill.

Evelyn Sullivan's spine stiffened instantly. As she turned, the belt of her bathrobe nearly whipped across Ethan's face. Recognition flickered in her eyes.

"How did you get in?"

His lips curled into a mocking smile. "Did I interrupt something important?" He took a step forward. "Or were you expecting someone else?"

Evelyn averted her gaze.

He seized her chin, forcing her to meet his eyes. "Answer me."

She slapped his hand away, the collar of her robe slipping slightly. "Your memory fails you, Mr. Sullivan. We agreed not to interfere in each other's lives." She adjusted her robe. "Who I wait for is none of your concern."

Ethan's eyes darkened, and a low chuckle escaped him.

"You're right." He leisurely undid his cufflinks. "I overstepped."

As Evelyn turned to leave, he pinned her against the wall.

The minty kiss stole her breath. Only when his scorching palm pressed against her lower back did she shove him away, gasping.

"Enough," she said, voice unsteady. "We're done for tonight."

Ethan arched a brow. "What exactly do you think just happened?"

Following her gaze to the scattered clothes on the floor, realization dawned. "You vomited on me. I just changed."

Evelyn finally noticed the faint scent of alcohol lingering in the air.

"Move. I need to shower."

"Together."

Before she could protest, he swept her into his arms. Skin met skin, sending a shiver through them both.

As water rose to her collarbone in the tub, Evelyn's ears burned red. "Get out!"

Ethan shrugged off his robe with one hand. "Might as well wash again."

His kiss was relentless, demanding. Evelyn resisted at first, but soon melted under his touch. Water sloshed over the tub's edge, splattering onto the tiles.

When he carried her back to bed, even her fingertips were flushed pink.

"Your hair's still wet," he said, reaching for the hairdryer.

Evelyn buried her face in the pillow. "Leave."

The warm air lulled her toward sleep—until the mattress dipped. She opened her eyes to find Ethan's intense gaze.

"Go to the guest room," she said coldly.

His expression hardened. "Throw me away after using me?"

She pulled the covers higher. "Don't forget, Mr. Sullivan. Ours is strictly a transactional relationship."

###Chapter 243

The air turned icy.

Ethan Sullivan's gaze was frigid, but Evelyn Sullivan met it with equal defiance. Neither would back down, and the bedroom temperature seemed to plummet.

Bang!

Ethan stormed out, the roar of his engine fading into the night.

Evelyn lay in bed, wide awake.

At dawn, she headed straight to the design competition venue.

"Sis?"

Isabella Jackson limped toward her, leaning on Victoria Farley's arm. Her smile was saccharine, but malice lurked in her eyes.

Evelyn ignored her.

"Disgraceful!" Victoria hissed through clenched teeth.

"Don't upset yourself, Mom," Isabella murmured. "What can you expect from someone raised in the countryside?"

Slap! Slap!

The sharp sound of two strikes echoed through the hall.

Isabella clutched her cheeks, stunned.

"Evelyn!" Victoria shrieked, raising her hand.

Evelyn caught her wrist in a vice grip. "Insult my foster parents again, and I'll make the Jacksons regret it."

"You?" Victoria sneered. "Ethan already threw you away!"

"Oh?" Evelyn's lips curved. "At Skyview Mansion, he didn't even spare you a glance."

Victoria's face darkened.

Isabella tugged her sleeve. "Mom, the competition's starting."

Inside the judging room, Evelyn had barely sat down when her phone rang.

"Have you seen my tie?" Ethan's voice came through the receiver.

###Chapter 244

"The password hasn't changed. You can check it yourself," Evelyn Sullivan said coolly.

"Fine."

The final round's theme was evening gown design, giving contestants ample creative freedom.

Designers worked with unprecedented focus, taking noticeably longer to complete their sketches. The first submission appeared on the judges' screens only after ninety minutes.

A black velvet slip dress with a V-neckline and delicate chain belt exuded effortless elegance in its simplicity.

Evelyn swiftly assigned scores and comments before uploading her evaluation.

Inside the venue, designers remained engrossed in their creations.

Isabella Jackson, her cast and crutches drawing frequent camera attention, crafted a rose-pink strapless gown. Twenty layers of tulle cascaded in a high-low hemline, the cinched waist lending ethereal movement.

Social media erupted instantly.

【This dress is everything! Mass-produce it NOW!】
【Isabella's got this in the bag. Crown her already!】
【Designing on crutches? Queen behavior!】

Isabella's follower count skyrocketed as official accounts flooded with praise.

Another hour passed before all submissions were finalized. Judges began scoring each entry individually.

Evelyn's efficiency proved staggering—she completed evaluations in under sixty minutes. While hailing a cab outside, Frank Ferguson's call interrupted her departure.

"Ms. Sullivan, I heard you've finished judging all entries?"

"Correct. Anything else?"

A pause. "There's something you should know... Isabella Jackson is competing."

"Current scores indicate she'll likely win."

Evelyn chuckled. "Not my concern."

The disconnected line left Frank sighing at his assistant. "Proceed with the original announcement."

Isabella ultimately claimed victory with 92.5 points. Victoria Farley immediately phoned William Jackson, demanding he spread the news to their entire social circle.
###Chapter 245

William Jackson's face glowed with excitement as he immediately instructed the butler to prepare a celebration banquet for that evening.

[Oh my god! Isabella actually won!]
[She's the pride of our domestic design industry!]
[But honestly, her work still lacks the depth of Elia's peak-era creations.]
[What do you know? Elia's been retired for years. Give Isabella time and she'll surpass her!]

The online debate grew increasingly heated.

The humble statement instantly garnered countless likes.

"Mom, let's invite Evelyn tonight," Isabella suddenly suggested.

Memories of Evelyn's actions made Victoria's chest heave with anger.

Isabella's fingers twitched.

Meanwhile, Evelyn Sullivan had just stepped through her front door when the design competition results notification arrived.

"I heard Isabella won?" Victoria's voice crackled through the receiver.

###Chapter 246

[Too scared to come home, sister? Afraid you'll pale in comparison?]

[Don't feel bad. After all those years in the countryside, it's natural you can't keep up.]

[If I were you, I'd leave Ethan voluntarily. Save him the shame.]

###Chapter 247

###Chapter 248

###Chapter 249

###Chapter 250

###Chapter 253

"I'll cover all company losses, Evelyn."

"I don't go out on weekends."

"Then we'll have a barbecue and watch movies at the villa."

It suddenly dawned on Evelyn that Ethan was planning a date. She immediately took a defensive step back. "I'm going home."

"This is your home."

"It's your villa."

"You like it? I'll transfer the deed to you right now."

"..."

Evelyn took a deep breath. "Mr. Sullivan, you know exactly what's wrong between us."

Ethan's gaze burned. "I prefer what you called me last night over 'Mr. Sullivan.'"

Every serious conversation got derailed by him. Furious, Evelyn turned to leave.

A hand suddenly closed around her wrist.

"Sophia says you've been working too hard lately," Ethan said, his voice low. "Take this weekend to relax."

"There's a bioluminescent jellyfish migration tonight. I'll take you home after."

The intensity in his dark eyes made Evelyn's heart skip.

She yanked her hand free. "You'd better keep your word."

When Ethan returned to the living room after finishing work, he found Evelyn curled in a corner of the sofa.

On screen, a ghostly pale woman was crawling out of a well—

"Ah!"

Evelyn grabbed the hands that suddenly covered her eyes and flipped their owner over her shoulder with a harsh thud.

She froze when she saw it was Ethan.

"Help me up," he ground out through clenched teeth.

"You shouldn't have sneaked up on me!" Evelyn retorted.

"You're scared of ghosts but you watch horror movies?"

"It's artistic appreciation!"

Ethan arched a brow. "Then who was trembling just now?"

Before he could finish, a grotesque face filled the screen.

Evelyn shrieked and threw herself into Ethan's arms.

"Artistic appreciation?" His chest vibrated with silent laughter.

"An accident!" She frantically turned off the TV.

As she tried to leave, an arm hooked around her waist and lifted her off her feet.

When his scorching kiss descended, Evelyn thought dazedly—he'd derailed her again...

The next afternoon.

Evelyn's face paled as she read Sophia's text.

"I'm leaving now," she said coldly, heading downstairs.

Ethan was preparing the barbecue in the courtyard. "At least stay for lunch."

"No need." Her grip tightened on her phone. "Any later and it'll be too late."

"What do you mean?"

Evelyn's smile was icy. "You deliberately kept me away so Isabella could steal my client?"

###Chapter 268

Ethan Sullivan's eyes turned icy. "What do you mean by that?"

Evelyn Sullivan's lips curled into a cold smile. "Am I wrong? Isabella couldn't have intercepted all my clients without your approval."

"Is that really how you see me?"

"Trust between us died long ago."

She turned and walked toward the street, her back rigid with resolve.

Thirty minutes later, Sophia Reynolds' red sports car pulled up in front of her.

"Get in." Sophia opened the passenger door. "It's worse than we thought."

Evelyn fastened her seatbelt. "Cut to the chase."

"Every potential client signed with Isabella." Sophia's grip tightened on the steering wheel. "And there's more... Brocade has been transferred to her name."

Evelyn's nails dug into her palms.

That dinner had been nothing but a trap.

"Ethan is ruthless." Sophia gritted her teeth. "If you hadn't returned when you did, MY Fashion Group would belong to Isabella by now."

"Take me home first." Evelyn closed her eyes briefly. "We'll rebuild our client base."

Sophia shot her a worried glance. "Do you want me to stay with you?"

"No."

As Evelyn stepped out of the car at her villa, she spotted Ethan waiting at the entrance.

"We need to talk." He blocked her path.

Evelyn unlocked the door without expression. "Come in."

Her detached demeanor stung him. "It's not what you think."

"Then what is it?" She turned to face him. "When your plan to acquire MY failed, you gave her Brocade as consolation?"

Ethan's pupils constricted. "You knew?"

"Does it matter?" She laughed lightly. "The show's over. Time to drop the act."

"If this was just an act, why would I go to Qingcheng to find you?!"

Her hand rested on the doorknob. "I've had enough of your games, Mr. Sullivan."

Ethan slammed his palm against the door. "I'll get to the bottom of this."

"Don't bother."

As the door clicked shut, she heard the sound of her own heart shattering.

###Chapter 269

Evelyn's gaze was icy, making Ethan's expression darken instantly.

"Evelyn, won't you even give me the most basic trust?"

As the door closed, her voice came through the wood.

"After the divorce, we should be strangers."

Ethan stood motionless for a moment before turning and driving away.

Meanwhile, Isabella received a call from Colin, saying Ethan wanted to see her. Overjoyed, she immediately began getting ready.

"Ethan, you wanted to see me?"

His cold stare pinned her in place. "What's going on with those distributors you signed?"

Her heart skipped a beat, but she forced calm. "Is there a problem?"

"Those same distributors were in talks with MY just days ago!"

Isabella shrugged. "Isn't business competition normal?"

His eyes turned glacial. "Tell me how you found them."

She paled. The contacts had come from an anonymous number, promising easy deals under the Sullivan name. What she thought was luck had backfired spectacularly.

"Someone... sent them to me anonymously..."

Ethan ordered Colin to investigate immediately. This was clearly an attack on MY—and possibly the Sullivans.

An hour later, Colin returned with a report.

"Sir, the trail leads to someone codenamed 'Scorpion.'"

"Background?"

"Former assassin guild member. Now operates independently against his old employers."

Ethan considered this. "Keep digging. Don't tell Evelyn yet."

For the next week, Evelyn was away on business, and their cold war continued.

On her return day, rain poured relentlessly.

Drenched, she reached the villa and spotted Ethan's car parked outside. She pretended not to see it, but footsteps followed as she unlocked the door.

Turning, she found him right behind her.

"Mr. Sullivan, I said—"

Before she could finish, she was yanked into a burning embrace.

###Chapter 270

"Ethan Sullivan, let go!"

Evelyn Sullivan's voice dripped with irritation as she shoved against the man before her. To her surprise, Ethan stumbled back easily this time.

Her breath caught when his towering frame suddenly pitched forward. Instinct made her grab his collar—the heat radiating from his skin burned her palm.

"You—"

Only then did she notice Ethan's tightly shut eyes and the unnatural flush staining his cheeks. She pressed her fingers to his forehead, jerking them back from the scalding temperature.

"Stop faking!" She slapped his face sharply, but got no response.

After a tense hesitation, she hauled him onto the sofa. The thermometer's reading made her stomach clench: 103.3°F.

"What a nuisance." Muttering, she forced antipyretics between his lips.

Colin Keller's voice crackled through the phone, strained with apology. "Ms. Sullivan, I'm out of town—"

Hanging up, Evelyn glared at the unconscious man before kicking the sofa leg.

"Did I owe you in a past life?"

Two hours later, Ethan's fever finally broke. As Evelyn turned toward the kitchen, a faint rustling stopped her.

The aroma of rice porridge filled the air. Ethan stirred awake, following the scent to the kitchen doorway. He leaned against the frame, drinking in the sight of her bustling figure.

"Awake?" Evelyn didn't turn around. "Wait in the living room."

"I want to watch you."

Her hands stilled briefly before resuming their work. She ignored the heat of his gaze—and the warmth creeping up her ears.

At the table, Ethan spoke suddenly. "Thank you."

"Don't." Evelyn set down her chopsticks. "Your ride's coming."

His utensils froze mid-air. "In such a hurry to get rid of me?"

"We ended things long ago."

Lightning split the sky outside, unleashing a torrential downpour. Ethan rose, his tall frame casting a shadow across the table.

"I'll visit another day."

"Don't bother."

The door clicked shut. Evelyn yanked open the curtains—watching his silhouette dissolve into the rain. She snapped them closed again, but couldn't shake the inexplicable ache in her chest.

One week later, Evelyn nearly dropped her champagne flute at a business gala. Her gaze snagged on a familiar figure surrounded by admirers.

Sophia Reynolds followed her stare, gasping. "Isn't that Mr. Sullivan?"

###Chapter 271

The gala sparkled with dazzling lights and clinking glasses. Evelyn Sullivan stood amidst the crowd, effortlessly charming several business partners. Her crimson V-neck dress accentuated her delicate collarbones, shimmering under the chandeliers.

"You're truly remarkable for your age, Ms. Sullivan. A toast to you." A partner raised his glass.

Evelyn lifted her champagne flute with grace, her red lips curving. "To our successful collaboration."

Just then, murmurs rippled through the entrance. Her peripheral vision caught Ethan Sullivan entering with Isabella Jackson on his arm. They looked like a perfect pair.

"Ethan, isn't that my sister?" Isabella feigned surprise, covering her lips. "Dressed like that while entertaining clients... How inappropriate."

Ethan's piercing gaze locked onto the striking figure in red. The effortless allure in her every movement drew admiring glances from the men around her. His fists clenched, knuckles turning white.

"Poor sister," Isabella sighed with faux sympathy. "Perhaps I could arrange a cushy position for her at Brocade?"

"Enough." Ethan's voice was glacial. "One more word against her, and our deal is off."

Isabella paled, her nails digging into her palms. She forced a smile. "I only meant to show concern—"

"She doesn’t need it." Ethan strode toward Evelyn, his back rigid with resolve.

Left behind, Isabella's eyes darkened with malice. Spotting Ryan Paisley nearby, his attention fixed on Evelyn, her lips twisted into a knowing smirk.

"How... interesting."

Evelyn was mid-conversation when an icy shiver ran down her spine. She turned to find Ethan approaching, and her brows instinctively furrowed.

"Mr. Sullivan!" The partner greeted him with flustered enthusiasm.

Ethan gave a curt nod. "I need a word with Ms. Sullivan."

Once alone, Evelyn dropped her polite facade and turned to leave.

"In such a hurry?" Ethan caught her wrist. "You seemed quite engaged earlier."

She wrenched free. "We have nothing to discuss, Mr. Sullivan."

"Sullivan Group has a project for MY."

"Not interested." Her voice was frosty. "Save it for Brocade."

He stepped closer. "What if it's personal?"

"Don’t you have better things to do?" She retreated, putting distance between them.

"For you? Always." His low voice carried a dangerous allure.

Evelyn scoffed and walked away without a backward glance, heading for the dessert table. As she picked up a slice of cake, a shadow fell over her.

"Ethan, must you—" She froze upon meeting Ryan Paisley's gaze instead. "Mr. Paisley?"

His expression was unreadable. "So you're the founder of MY."

###Chapter 272

Evelyn Sullivan noticed the peculiar look in Ryan Paisley's eyes, but she had long been prepared to reveal her identity.

"Something wrong?"

A flicker of complex emotions passed through Ryan's gaze. "My apologies. I didn't realize you were the CEO of MY."

Evelyn frowned slightly, sensing an underlying meaning in his words.

"No need for formalities, Mr. Paisley. Business is business."

Ryan's expression dimmed. "If the opportunity arises, I'll prioritize working with MY in the future."

Evelyn arched a brow in surprise, about to respond politely when a cold voice cut in from behind.

"Having a pleasant chat?"

Without turning, she replied, "None of your concern."

Ethan Sullivan sat beside her with a dark expression, replacing her wine glass with warm milk.

"Drink less."

Too tired to argue, Evelyn stirred the milk absently.

"Ryan, you have other matters to attend to," Ethan dismissed him outright.

Ryan gave Evelyn one last lingering look before walking away.

"Stay away from him," Ethan said abruptly.

Evelyn scoffed. "What? Afraid I'll seduce your friend?"

Before Ethan could respond, Sophia Reynolds rushed over in a flurry.

"Evelyn, Mr. Wang and the others are waiting."

Grateful for the escape, Evelyn stood immediately.

Only when they turned the corner did Sophia lower her voice. "Ethan parades Isabella around like some trophy, then comes crawling back to you. Does he think he's some emperor picking concubines?"

"That's not the right idiom," Evelyn sighed, rubbing her temples.

"That's what you're focusing on?!" Sophia stomped her foot. "He's humiliating you!"

Evelyn's gaze drifted to the mingling crowd in the distance, her fingers unconsciously digging into her palms.

"I know my limits."

By the end of the gala, Evelyn was slightly tipsy. Sophia anxiously instructed the designated driver before watching her leave.

Through the car window, neon lights blurred into streaks. Leaning back, Evelyn let her thoughts wander into the night.

###Chapter 273 

Ryan Paisley had just stepped into the underground parking lot when he spotted Isabella Jackson leaning against his black Maybach. Her beige trench coat stood out starkly under the dim lighting.

"Mr. Paisley, there are a few clauses in the Brocade contract I don't quite understand." Isabella tucked a loose strand of hair behind her ear, offering a perfectly calculated smile.

Ryan expressionlessly pulled out his car keys. "Take it to Legal."

She suddenly stepped forward, her heels clicking sharply against the concrete. "Or we could talk about my sister. I heard you—"

"Enough!" Ryan whirled around, his gaze sharp as a blade. "Don't mention her in front of me."

The next morning, Sophia Reynolds burst into Evelyn Sullivan's office, waving a document.

"Paisley Group offered us a partnership! They're giving us their prime retail space!"

Evelyn's pen froze mid-signature, leaving a small blue ink blot on the paper. "Decline it."

"Are you insane? That's prime real estate!" Sophia slammed the file onto the desk. "It could boost our sales by 80%!"

Evelyn looked up, sunlight filtering through the blinds to cast fragmented shadows across her face. "Ryan Paisley and Ethan Sullivan grew up together."

"So what?" Sophia braced her hands on the desk. "Business is war. Why turn down free profit?"

Evelyn eventually relented but insisted on personally inviting Ryan to dinner as thanks.

When the call connected, Ryan was reviewing documents. At the sound of Evelyn's voice, his pen dragged a long line across the page.

"Seven tonight, Royal View Steakhouse." Her voice carried through the receiver. "Are you available, Mr. Paisley?"

His Adam's apple bobbed. "I am."

After hanging up, he rose and walked to the floor-to-ceiling window. Sunlight caught the faint upward curve of his lips.

The moment of quiet was shattered by Ethan's call.

"What's this about Brocade's storefront?" Ethan's voice was glacial.

Ryan watched the steady stream of traffic below. "It better suits MY's needs."

The sound of crumpling paper came through the line. "Stay away from her." Each word was enunciated with lethal precision before the call abruptly ended.

Ryan tossed his phone onto the sofa. His tie suddenly felt suffocating. He loosened the knot, his eyes dark with unreadable emotion.

###Chapter 274

"Understood."

Ethan Sullivan set down his phone, his long fingers tapping twice on the desk. He lifted his gaze to Colin Keller standing nearby, his voice low. "Inform Isabella that the Paisley Group has chosen another partner."

Colin nodded and turned to make the arrangements.

Isabella Jackson was reviewing documents in her office when the news reached her. Her fountain pen jerked to a halt, ink bleeding across the paper. She slowly raised her head, her eyes dark and venomous as she stared at her secretary. "Find out. Who did the Paisleys choose?"

Thirty minutes later, the secretary nervously handed her the investigative report.

"MY?" Isabella let out a cold laugh, her nails digging deep into her palms. She snatched her phone and dialed Ryan Paisley's number, her voice sickly sweet. "Mr. Paisley, is this your way of taunting me?"

A derisive snort came through the line.

"You overestimate your importance, Ms. Jackson," Ryan's voice was icy. "Business is business. It's all about capability."

Isabella narrowed her eyes, her red lips parting. "Aren't you afraid I'll expose your feelings for Evelyn—"

"Isabella." Ryan cut her off sharply, his tone dangerous. "If you dare breathe a word, I'll make sure you never set foot in Rongcheng again."

The call ended abruptly.

Crack! Her brand-new phone shattered against the wall. Isabella's chest heaved violently, her eyes burning with hatred.

She would make Evelyn pay.

At six in the evening, Evelyn pushed open the glass door of the restaurant. Ryan was already seated by the window and stood immediately when he saw her.

"Sorry, rush hour traffic was terrible."

Ryan smiled warmly. "I was just early."

The candlelit dinner was pleasant. Ryan was witty, drawing soft laughter from Evelyn behind her hand. Neither noticed the camera lens trained on them from a corner table.

"Let me drive you home," Ryan offered as they settled the bill.

They had just stepped outside when a black Maybach screeched to a halt at the curb. The window rolled down, revealing Ethan's sharp profile.

"Get in."

Evelyn froze. "How did you—"

"Sophia told me," Ethan said flatly.

Evelyn frowned skeptically. Sophia, with her fiery temper, would voluntarily contact Ethan?

"That's not necessary. I can—"

"It's about the divorce," Ethan interrupted, his voice low.

Evelyn pressed her lips together, then turned to Ryan with an apologetic smile. "Thank you for dinner."

Before Ryan could respond, Ethan stepped between them. The two men locked eyes, tension crackling in the air.

"Ryan," Ethan's voice was glacial. "Stay away from her."

Ryan remained unruffled. "You're crossing a line, Ethan."

The car door slammed shut. The Maybach roared away, leaving Ryan standing in its wake, his expression darkening as he watched the taillights disappear.

###Chapter 275

The car door slammed shut. Ethan Sullivan's face was icy as he ordered the driver to go.

The black Maybach merged into traffic. He turned to glare at Evelyn Sullivan, his eyes dark. "I warned you to stay away from Ryan Paisley."

"Mr. Sullivan, MY Fashion Group has business dealings with Paisley Corp. Having dinner with him is perfectly normal." Evelyn smirked. "Should I pretend not to know him when we meet?"

Ethan's jaw tightened. After a moment of silence, he spoke. "That's not what I meant."

"Your meaning doesn't matter." Evelyn stared straight ahead. "Last night you said we needed to talk. About what?"

"About what you proposed. I want you to reconsider."

Evelyn frowned. "There's nothing to reconsider. You and I—"

Before she could finish, Ethan suddenly cupped the back of her head and crushed his lips against hers.

Caught off guard, Evelyn struggled, but he held her firmly. The kiss was relentless, leaving her breathless by the time he finally pulled away.

"You still feel something for me." Ethan brushed his thumb over her swollen lips. "Why won't you give us another chance?"

Evelyn shoved him away, her eyes clear and cold. "So what if I do? You and Isabella Jackson are always tangled up together. I won't make the same mistake again."

"There's nothing between us."

"Nothing? Then why do you take her to every event? Why let everyone think she's your girlfriend?" Evelyn's lips curled in mockery. "Ethan, don't treat me like a fool."

His gaze darkened. "Some things can't be explained right now. But I swear, Isabella and I will never be together."

"Save your lies for someone else."

"I'll prove it to you."

Silence filled the car. When it stopped in front of the villa, Evelyn turned to him before getting out. "Don't waste your effort, Mr. Sullivan. Nothing you do means anything to me now."

She'd given him too many chances in those three years. It was too late now.

Ethan clenched his fists as he watched her walk away without looking back.

For the next few days, Ethan didn't appear again. But the entertainment pages were flooded with photos of him and Isabella. Soon, news broke that Isabella had been appointed CEO of Brocade.

"Making it look like a coronation," Sophia Reynolds muttered, flipping through the headlines.

Evelyn raised a brow. "You really dislike her, don't you?"

"I've hated her fake act since we were kids! Now I hate her even more for scheming against you." Sophia snorted. "She's just a fraud propped up by Sullivan Group."

"Don't underestimate her." Evelyn handed her a file. "Brocade has Sullivan Group's backing. We need to stay sharp."

Sophia took the file. "With you here, we won't lose to that impostor!"

"We've lost before." Evelyn chuckled.

"Only because Sullivan Group interfered!" Sophia fumed. "That's all she's good for."

Meanwhile, in Simon Reynolds' office...

"Brother, are you ready?" he asked into the phone, his tone deceptively gentle.

The voice on the other end wavered. "Simon, I'm still scared carrying this fake bomb..."

"Relax, it's just mud inside." Simon's eyes turned cold. "Think about how Sophia abandoned you. If Evelyn hadn't poisoned her against you, she wouldn't have left you to rot."

"But—"

"I paid off all your gambling debts. Would I really harm you?" Simon lowered his voice. "We're just scaring her a little—making her back off."

###Chapter 276

Samuel Reynolds' hand trembled slightly as he gripped his phone. Silence stretched between both ends of the call.

"Fine. I'll do as you say."

Simon Reynolds' sinister chuckle came through the line. "Big brother, opportunities are fleeting. Miss this one, and the next won't be so easy."

"Understood."

After hanging up, Simon slammed his phone onto the desk, eyes glinting with cold fury.

Evelyn Sullivan, you brought this upon yourself.

At exactly 3 PM, Quincy Howard burst into the CEO's office, face pale.

"Ms. Sullivan! There's a madman downstairs with a bomb—he's demanding to see you!"

Evelyn shot to her feet, sending documents scattering. "What? Do we know who it is?"

"Not yet, but it's too dangerous! The police are on their way—"

"We can't wait!" Evelyn strode toward the elevator. "What about the reception?"

Quincy's voice shook. "He...he's taken the receptionist hostage..."

Evelyn froze mid-step, her gaze turning razor-sharp. "Why didn't you say so sooner?"

As the elevator doors opened, she saw an unexpected figure.

"Sophia? Get out of here now!"

Samuel suddenly lunged forward, glaring at Evelyn. "You're the bitch who turned my family against me!"

Sophia's eyes reddened with panic. "Dad! Do you realize what you're doing?!"

"Shut up!" Samuel tightened his grip on the hostage with a vicious grin. "Today, this woman pays the price!"

Evelyn noticed the hostage swaying unsteadily and spoke calmly, "Let her go. Take me instead."

Meanwhile, live footage of the scene was spreading like wildfire online.

At Sullivan Group's headquarters, Colin Keller stumbled into the conference room.

"Mr. Sullivan! MY is under attack!"

Ethan Sullivan's heart nearly stopped when he saw the familiar figure on screen. Grabbing his jacket, he bolted for the door—only to have his calls repeatedly rejected.

[Evelyn! Fall back immediately!]
[The bomb is real!]
[Answer me!]

His messages vanished into the void. On the surveillance feed, Evelyn was steadily approaching the madman.

"No tricks!" Samuel barked.

Evelyn's trained eyes instantly assessed the explosive device at his waist—powerful enough to level the entire floor.

"Relax," she slowly raised her hands. "I'm just an unarmed woman."

###Chapter 277

Samuel Reynolds curled his lips into a sinister smirk. "Be smart. Hands up and come here to exchange places!"

Evelyn Sullivan slowly raised her arms and stepped toward him. The entire lobby fell silent. Everyone held their breath, their eyes locked on Samuel's finger hovering over the detonator.

After three steps, Sophia Reynolds suddenly rushed forward and grabbed Evelyn's wrist.

"Evelyn, don't go!"

Sophia turned to Samuel, her eyes blazing with fury. "Dad, when will this end?! Do you really want to ruin my life?!"

Samuel sneered. "If it weren't for her poisoning your mind, you wouldn't have abandoned your own father! Everything that's happened to me is her fault! Once she's dead, you'll come back to me!"

"You're insane! Fine, if you want to die, I'll die with you!"

Sophia lunged at him.

Samuel staggered back, dragging the receptionist with him, panic flashing in his eyes. "Stop! One more step and I'll blow us all up!"

Evelyn yanked Sophia back. "He's unstable. Don't provoke him. Since he wants me, I'll talk to him. Once the receptionist is safe, evacuate everyone to the floors above the sixth. Ideally, get them out of the building entirely."

Sophia shook her head desperately, tears welling. "No, let me go instead."

"He won't agree." Evelyn lowered her voice. "I think someone's pulling his strings."

Sophia's pupils constricted. "What do you—"

"What are you whispering about?!" Samuel barked. "Evelyn, you have thirty seconds! Come here or we all die!"

"Remember what I said." Evelyn gave Sophia's hand a reassuring squeeze and walked toward Samuel.

Watching the unrecognizable madness in her father's eyes, Sophia felt her heart shatter. The man who had once carried her on his shoulders to watch fireworks and brought her dolls was gone—just like the Reynolds Corporation.

"Let her go," Evelyn said, stopping in front of Samuel.

He shoved the receptionist away. "Turn around!"

When Evelyn didn't move, he brandished the detonator. "Now! Or I'll send us all to hell!"

Evelyn slowly turned. Cold metal pressed against the back of her neck.

Sophia seized the moment, helping the trembling receptionist flee.

"Who said you could leave?!" Samuel roared.

"You wanted me," Evelyn said calmly. "Let them go. I'm staying."

"Shut up! If it weren't for you, Sophia's money would already be mine!"

"And?"

Samuel faltered. He'd only meant to intimidate Evelyn into forcing Sophia's compliance—not face this unnerving composure.

"You're not afraid to die?!" He jammed the gun harder against her skull.

Evelyn chuckled. "Terrified. But what good would that do? Though I doubt you really want to die for someone else's agenda."

The words ignited him. "Shut your mouth! If I die, you're coming with me!"

He slammed his thumb down on the detonator.

Beep.

The display on his chest lit up. Crimson numbers began their relentless countdown:

30:00.

###Chapter 278

The grand hall plunged into dead silence.

Every eye froze on the flashing red numbers strapped to Samuel Reynolds' chest. The air turned glacial.

Sophia Reynolds' face drained of color, her lips trembling uncontrollably.

"Transfer the money now, Sophia!" Samuel snarled, his fingers digging into Evelyn Sullivan's shoulder. "Or we all die together!"

Evelyn suddenly laughed.

"What's so funny?!" Samuel's grip tightened violently.

Samuel's pupils contracted sharply.

"What are you implying?"

Her words were cut off by rapid footsteps.

Ethan Sullivan's imposing figure appeared in the doorway, his tailored suit immaculate, his expression stormy.

"Release her."

Three words that made the temperature in the hall plummet.

Samuel's hands began shaking. "M-Mr. Sullivan..."

Evelyn felt Samuel's entire body stiffen behind her.

"Impossible..." Samuel muttered. "He said this was just a performance..."

Evelyn seized on the slip. "Who said that? Simon Reynolds?"

Samuel's eyes widened comically at being exposed.

Suddenly, the bomb's countdown accelerated with an ear-piercing beep.

"Two minutes left." Evelyn announced coolly. "Convinced now?"

Beads of sweat formed on Samuel's forehead as his entire frame shook violently.

"N-no... this can't be..."

Ethan strode forward.

"Stay back!" Samuel scrambled away in panic.

"One minute." Ethan continued advancing. "Either let me disarm it, or we all die here."

Evelyn stared at Ethan in shock.

He knew bomb disposal?

Samuel finally collapsed, knees hitting the marble floor. "D-disarm it! Quickly!"

Ethan moved like lightning. His long fingers expertly opened the bomb's casing.

The timer froze at 00:23.

Not a sound could be heard in the hall. Everyone held their breath.

A soft click echoed.

Ethan tossed the detached detonator aside and fixed his gaze on the crumpled figure of Samuel.

"Now. We settle accounts."

###Chapter 279

Evelyn Sullivan withdrew her hand with cold indifference. "Suit yourself."

Samuel Reynolds' forehead glistened with sweat. He'd only intended to extort money from Sophia, not gamble with his life.

Ethan Sullivan glanced at the timer, his voice icy. "Eighteen minutes left. The bomb squad won't make it."

"Then... I'm dead?"

Samuel's eyes flashed with venom. "If I die, you're all coming with me!"

Evelyn lowered her gaze, considering. "I can disarm it."

"How do I know you're not trying to kill me?"

She nearly laughed at his stupidity. "I'll be right beside you. If it blows, we all go."

His Adam's apple bobbed as he hesitated.

"Well?" Evelyn checked the timer impatiently. "Keep wasting time and everyone dies."

"Fine... Fine! Do it!"

A deep voice cut in.

"I'll help."

Evelyn frowned at Ethan. "Stay out of this!"

Bomb disposal left no room for error. She wouldn't risk him.

He stepped beside her anyway.

"Don't be afraid. I'm here."

"I said no!" Her glare could freeze lava. "Get out now!"

"I know some bomb mechanics."

"I don't need—"

"Fifteen minutes left." Ethan watched the timer. "Keep arguing?"

Her jaw clenched. "Your funeral."

When the scissors arrived, only the three remained in the hall. Samuel's legs shook—he finally believed the bomb was real.

Each tick echoed like Death's footsteps. Beads of sweat formed on Evelyn's brow. The device was simple, but every wire glowed crimson.

With two wires remaining, time nearly expired.

"Do you even know what you're doing?!" Samuel's voice trembled.

"Shut up!"

Evelyn inhaled sharply and turned to Ethan. "Step back."

Once he retreated to safety, she gripped the scissors.

Snip.

One red wire severed.

###Chapter 280

The bomb's countdown suddenly stopped, plunging the space into eerie silence.

Evelyn Sullivan and Samuel Reynolds exchanged glances, their tense nerves beginning to relax—until a piercing beep shattered the quiet.

The red numbers began flashing wildly.

A pair of strong hands suddenly grabbed the bomb and sprinted outside.

"Ethan!"

Evelyn's scream tore through the air as she stumbled after him, catching only a glimpse of his retreating figure.

Boom—

The deafening explosion sent her flying backward.

In the last moment before darkness claimed her, all she saw was Ethan being swallowed by flames.

"Evelyn!"

Sophia Reynolds' frantic voice jolted Evelyn awake. The sharp scent of disinfectant stung her nose as she realized she was in a hospital.

"Where's Ethan?" She yanked out her IV, blood trickling down her hand.

Sophia quickly restrained her. "He's in the next room. His injuries are serious, but—"

Before she could finish, Evelyn was already barefoot and running.

Her heart nearly stopped when she pushed open the door.

Ethan sat propped up in bed, crimson seeping through the bandage at his temple. Hearing the noise, he lifted his head slowly, his deep eyes reflecting her disheveled state.

Evelyn threw herself into his arms, her trembling fingers clutching his hospital gown.

"You scared me to death..." Hot tears soaked through the fabric.

Ethan stiffened for a moment before gently wrapping his arms around her slender shoulders. "I'm okay."

"I'm sorry... I dragged you into this again."

"I did it willingly."

Evelyn pulled back, her red-rimmed eyes locking onto his. "Ethan, let's start over."

The air froze.

His Adam's apple bobbed. "Don't pity me."

"I want to be with you." Her voice was soft but clear. "When that bomb went off, I finally understood."

After a long silence, Ethan finally cupped her face. "Okay."

Evelyn smiled through her tears, only then noticing her bare feet. Ethan frowned and lifted her onto the bed, his warm hands enveloping her icy toes.

"Ethan!"

A shrill voice shattered the moment. Isabella Jackson stood in the doorway, her meticulously applied makeup unable to mask her twisted expression.

Ethan didn't even glance up. "Get out."

"I came to visit—"

"Do I need to repeat myself?"

Isabella's gaze burned into their joined hands before she finally slammed the door. As the glass rattled, Evelyn secretly hooked her pinky around Ethan's.

###Chapter 281

Isabella Jackson's beautiful eyes burned with venom as she shot Evelyn Sullivan one last glare before leaving.

Ethan Sullivan moved to approach, but Evelyn shoved him away.

"Wasn't the great Mr. Sullivan always so tender toward delicate flowers?" Her lips curled in mockery. "Why so cold to your First Love now?"

He chuckled low, his thumb grazing the delicate skin of her wrist.

"Jealous?"

"Don't flatter yourself." She wrenched her hand free. "I'm just curious when your tastes changed."

Suddenly, his hand cradled the back of her head, his breath scorching against her skin.

"Now."

Before she could react, his lips captured hers in a searing kiss. Evelyn struggled briefly before melting into its intensity.

"Bastard..." she gasped when they finally parted.

Ethan nuzzled her flushed cheek with his nose.

"Now do you know who I want?"

She turned her face away. "I can let the past go. But from now on, if you dare have even the slightest connection with Isabella—"

Her words were cut off as his mouth claimed hers again.

"As you wish, Mrs. Sullivan," he murmured against her lips, amusement lacing his rough voice.

At the mention of Samuel Reynolds, Ethan's gaze turned icy.

"The police are interrogating him. But..." He paused. "The mastermind won't stay quiet for long."

Evelyn's eyes flashed.

"Simon Reynolds?"

Ethan arched a brow. "Seems we're on the same page."

He pressed a kiss to her hair. "Leave this to me. Focus on recovering."

Meanwhile, a loud crash echoed through the office at Sullivan Corp.

"Useless! Can't even handle a woman!" Simon Reynolds kicked over a coffee table and grabbed his phone. "Arrange a meeting with Samuel immediately!"

Outside MY Fashion Group, bystanders swarmed the explosion site, phones raised to capture the chaos.

The hashtag #SullivanProtectsHisWife rocketed to the top of trending.

[Shocking! Ethan Sullivan's wife is actually Evelyn Sullivan?!]

[Rich people drama! Wasn't he always parading her sister around?]

[Wrong focus! This is the second bombing!]

[Waiting for the catfight!]

Evelyn hurled her phone at Ethan's chest.

"Calculating as always, Mr. Sullivan. Still tying me to you after divorce?"

He calmly locked the screen.

"It was an emergency."

"Issue a clarification statement now!"

In one swift motion, he pinned her to the hospital bed, his breath hot against her ear.

"Darling, do you really think anyone would believe it now?"

The door burst open.

Lucas Laurier's fruit basket hit the floor with a thud.

"You two...reconciled?"

Ethan didn't release her, tightening his embrace instead.

"As you see." His challenging gaze lingered on the stunned trio in the doorway, especially Ryan Paisley.

###Chapter 282

"Let go or I'll really get angry!" Evelyn Sullivan's cheeks burned crimson as she pushed against Ethan Sullivan's chest.

The tips of her ears turned pink. Only then did Ethan release her with an amused smile.

The moment she was free, Evelyn leaped off the bed. She fled in such a hurry that she even stepped into Ethan's slippers. She didn't stop to greet Lucas Laurier and the others waiting in the living room.

"Tsk tsk. Bad timing, huh?" Lucas leaned against the doorframe with a teasing grin.

Ethan calmly adjusted his hospital gown. "Then leave."

"Prioritizing love over friendship!" Lucas shook his head with a laugh.

Ryan Paisley suddenly spoke up. "You two made up?"

"Yes."

Ethan's gaze lifted to meet his. The temperature in the room instantly dropped.

Ryan's throat moved as he silently looked away. He thought his chance had finally come. Turns out it was just false hope.

"Let's go." Sensing the tension, Lucas was the first to turn around.

Once they left, Ethan dialed Colin Keller. "Find out who's behind Samuel Reynolds."

...

In the visitation room, Samuel Reynolds stared blankly at his brother Simon Reynolds across the table.

The moment those explosives detonated, he knew this brother never considered him family.

"Simon. I knew you'd come." In the end, Samuel chose silence. His ungrateful daughter Sophia was unreliable. His only hope now was this brother.

An unspoken agreement passed between them—Simon would pull strings outside while Samuel kept his mouth shut.

Exiting the police station, Simon exhaled deeply. He called Sophia, his voice icy. "Come to my place."

Thirty minutes later, Sophia stood in his living room.

"Just say it, Uncle."

Simon sighed. "Your father's too old for prison. You're close with Evelyn..."

"You want me to beg for leniency?" Sophia let out a cold laugh. "He nearly killed two people!"

"He's your father!"

Sophia clenched her fists. "The day my mother jumped off that building, I became fatherless."

As she turned to leave, she didn't see Simon retrieving the recorder hidden under the coffee table.

He never intended to save his gambling addict brother. But Samuel needed to know—no one else would care about a failed murderer except him.

###Chapter 283

Evelyn Sullivan and Ethan Sullivan's injuries weren't severe, so they were discharged quickly.

"Move into Imperial Court with me." Ethan stood at the hospital room door, his tone leaving no room for refusal.

Evelyn packed her belongings without looking up. "Fine. But I take the guest room."

His brow furrowed slightly before he relented.

The move went smoothly. Evelyn wheeled her suitcase into the guest room and locked the door behind her.

The aroma of food drifted from the living room.

"Did you order takeout?" She eyed the elaborate spread of four dishes and soup on the dining table, surprised.

Ethan was setting the table. "Eat first."

Over dinner, Evelyn picked at the steamed sea bass. "Any progress with Samuel Reynolds?"

"He insists the bombing was his idea alone." Ethan ladled soup into her bowl. "But Simon Reynolds paid off his five-million gambling debt."

She smirked. "No wonder he's so loyal."

After dinner, Ethan's phone rang. Glancing at the caller ID, he excused himself to the study.

"Mr. Sullivan, should we continue pursuing the Brocade project?" Colin Keller's voice came through the receiver.

Ethan stood by the window, the night casting shadows on his sharp profile. "Withdraw as soon as Isabella Jackson takes over."

Hanging up, he massaged his temples. He needed to fulfill those three conditions with Isabella quickly.

Meanwhile, Isabella stared at her phone screen, face darkening.

"Sullivan Group is pulling funding?" She hurled her phone onto the couch. "Evelyn, this is your doing again!"

With trembling fingers, she dialed Margaret Sullivan, voice quivering. "Aunt Margaret, there's something important you should know..."

In an upscale café's private room, Isabella stirred her latte.

"My sister wasn't lost as a child," she whispered. "My parents abandoned her on purpose."

Margaret's spoon clattered against the saucer.

"A feng shui master claimed she'd bring ruin to the Jackson family." Isabella's eyes gleamed strangely. "That master died suddenly soon after."

Margaret returned to the Sullivan estate shaking uncontrollably.

"What's wrong?" Henry Sullivan set aside his newspaper.

"Remember Master Zhang who did our feng shui readings?" Her voice trembled. "He was right—Evelyn is a jinx!"

Henry's expression darkened. "Nonsense!"

"The Jacksons knew it, that's why they discarded her!" Margaret stood abruptly. "Ever since Ethan married her, our family's been plagued with misfortune!"

Outside, lightning split the night sky.

###Chapter 284

Henry Sullivan's gaze was sharp as a blade, sweeping coldly over Margaret Sullivan's face.

"Instead of being paranoid all day, why don't you go out and relax?" He adjusted his suit cuff. "I have a meeting at the company."

Margaret grabbed his arm.

"Ethan must cut ties with Evelyn Sullivan completely! That woman will be the death of him!"

"Don't be ridiculous!" Henry shook off her hand. "Adrian just joined the company. Ethan already has enough on his plate."

Flames of anger burned in Margaret's eyes.

"Henry Sullivan! All you care about is the company. Do you even care if your son lives or dies?"

"Suit yourself."

He walked toward the elevator without looking back.

"Stop right there!"

The elevator doors slid shut, reflecting her distorted image.

This business marriage had long been a hollow shell. After giving birth to twins, Henry never stepped into her bedroom again. Years of hysterical arguments had only resulted in icy civility.

Ethan was her only pride.

She would never let anyone ruin him.

Confronting Ethan directly wouldn’t work. She needed another plan.

Evelyn Sullivan had just stepped into her office when Simon Reynolds blocked the doorway.

"President Sullivan, for Sophia's sake, let my brother go."

She set her bag on the desk without glancing up.

"Are you pleading for a murderer?"

"He was just following orders! Sophia has already lost her mother. She can’t lose her father too!"

Evelyn suddenly smiled.

"You seem to be missing the point."

"What do you mean?"

"This is a criminal case." She lifted her gaze. "No one involved will escape justice—including the mastermind."

Simon's face paled.

"Don’t push this too far!"

"Save that speech for the judge." Evelyn flipped open a file. "By the way, starting today, you’ll handle customer service. I’m taking over the fabric division."

"You can’t just demote me!"

"Twenty-three percent complaint rate, Mr. Reynolds." She twirled a pen. "Focus on improving service quality."

Simon slammed the door so hard the glass rattled.

Unfazed, Evelyn picked up the intercom. "Replace this with a soundproof door."

As evening fell, her phone lit up with Ethan’s call.

"Grandmother wants us to have dinner at Harmony Manor."

Evelyn’s fingers stilled.

"She knows?"

"I told her."

"..."

"Not happy?"

She rubbed her temples. "You couldn’t wait, could you?"

"We can reschedule if you don’t want to go."

"No need." She glanced at her lipstick. "Pick me up after work."

After hanging up, she pressed her lips together in the mirror.

The rose-tinted gloss shimmered under the light.

###Chapter 285

The elevator doors slid open, revealing Sophia Reynolds standing directly in Evelyn Sullivan's path.

Sophia's eyes swept over Evelyn with an amused smirk.

"My, my. Someone's glowing today. Ethan must be treating you well."

Evelyn's ears turned pink. She shot her friend an indignant glare.

"Stop talking nonsense!"

Sophia blinked innocently.

"I merely meant you two have reconciled. Your mind went somewhere else, didn't it?"

Evelyn fell silent.

Leaning closer, Sophia lowered her voice. "That blush... Did something happen last night—"

"Director Reynolds!" Evelyn gritted her teeth. "Seems like your workload isn't heavy enough."

Sophia immediately raised her hands in surrender. "I'm off to work overtime!"

As they walked toward the lobby together, Evelyn suddenly remembered something.

"Is Alexander still bothering you?"

"Rejected him ages ago." Sophia waved a hand dismissively. "I'm seeing someone new now."

Evelyn's eyes lit up. "Who?"

"Top secret." Sophia flashed a mysterious smile. "I'll introduce you when things are more serious."

Outside the building, Ethan's Maybach waited by the curb.

Evelyn opened the car door to find a bouquet of sunflowers resting on the seat.

"You remembered these are my favorite?"

Ethan kept his eyes on the road. "The vase in our living room never runs out of them."

That simple statement warmed Evelyn's heart.

At Harmony Manor, a gray Rolls-Royce stood out conspicuously.

Inside, Adrian Sullivan was entertaining Grandma Sullivan with jokes.

His smile faded slightly when he saw them enter.

"I'll let you spend time with Grandma. I need some air in the garden."

As he passed by, Evelyn distinctly felt the weight of his lingering gaze.

Grandma Sullivan grasped Evelyn's hand tightly. "You've really made up?"

Ethan opened his mouth to speak, but Grandma cut him off with a glare.

"No one asked you! If this girl suffers again, you'll answer to me first!"

"Grandma..." Ethan's expression darkened.

Evelyn suppressed a laugh and intervened. "He's been good to me lately."

Grandma snorted. "He'd better be!"

Ethan pinched the bridge of his nose impassively.

Evelyn secretly squeezed his hand before turning back. "How is Adrian adjusting at Sullivan Corp?"

###Chapter 286

Ethan's eyes darkened slightly. His fingers tapped twice on the armrest.

"Passable."

Grandma Sullivan sighed, fine wrinkles forming at the corners of her eyes. "Adrian is struggling right now. After all, he's your cousin..."

She turned away before finishing.

Ethan's expression remained unchanged. "As long as he behaves."

The position of Sullivan Group's CEO should have been Adrian's.

After that car accident years ago, Adrian fled overseas.

It was Ethan who single-handedly built Sullivan Group into what it was today.

"Once he's settled, I'll provide him with startup funds," Grandma Sullivan murmured, tracing the rim of her teacup. "Look out for him."

"Mhm."

The study lights burned late into the night.

Grandma Sullivan clasped Evelyn's hand, her palm warm. "Thank you for giving him another chance, dear."

She often wished Evelyn was her own granddaughter.

"Grandma, the future is unpredictable."

"If that boy messes up again, I'll be the first to skin him alive."

Evelyn's eyes grew moist.

"By the way," Grandma Sullivan suddenly lowered her voice, "do you know any suitable young ladies?"

"For Adrian?"

"His parents are gone. I worry about him."

Evelyn thought for a moment. "How about throwing a welcome banquet?"

Grandma Sullivan's eyes lit up. "This weekend!"

Under the chandelier's glow, four people sat with hidden thoughts.

Adrian remained silent throughout, only giving curt replies when Grandma spoke.

When Evelyn glanced at him for the third time, Ethan abruptly set down his fork.

The car ride home was suffocatingly tense.

"Mr. Sullivan?" Evelyn poked his rigid profile. "Who pissed you off?"

###Chapter 287

Ethan Sullivan's eyes turned icy, his voice laced with bitterness.

"At dinner, your gaze was practically glued to Adrian Sullivan. Anyone would think you two were the couple."

Evelyn Sullivan couldn't help but laugh, tilting her head. "You're upset over that?"

"Isn't that enough?"

"More than enough." She smiled, explaining, "Grandmother wanted me to introduce him to potential girlfriends. I suggested hosting a welcome banquet to invite socialites from Rongcheng."

Ethan snorted. "Welcome banquet? More like a matchmaking event."

Evelyn fell silent.

After a pause, she ventured, "You seem to have issues with Adrian?"

"I don't." He turned away. "I just don't like him."

Noticing his dark expression, Evelyn wisely dropped the subject.

When they returned to Imperial Court, Margaret Sullivan was waiting.

Spotting Evelyn, Margaret's eyes dimmed, clearly surprised they had reconciled.

Evelyn nodded politely. "I'll head to my room."

"Wait." Margaret suddenly stopped her, smiling warmly. "I brought dumplings. Freeze them, and you can cook them whenever you like."

Evelyn hesitated before accepting the insulated box, puzzled by Margaret's sudden kindness.

"Thank you, Mrs. Sullivan."

Margaret patted her hand. "I was too stubborn before. Your relationship is your business. I shouldn't interfere."

After seeing Margaret out, Evelyn turned—only to be pinned against the refrigerator by Ethan.

"Eth—"

His lips crushed hers before she could finish.

Clutching his collar, Evelyn arched into the kiss.

He only pulled away when she gasped for air.

"Move into the master bedroom tonight."

"No." She was firm. "We agreed on separate rooms."

He studied her determined gaze before sighing. "Fine."

As Evelyn turned to leave, he yanked her back.

"Compensation."

Their heated kiss was interrupted by a ringing phone.

Ethan checked the caller ID. "Work emergency. I have to go."

"Go ahead."

He gave her a long look before turning—only to freeze when she suddenly called out, "Wait!"

His back stiffened, fingers clenching unconsciously.

###Chapter 288

Evelyn rose on her toes, her slender fingers smoothing the wrinkles from Ethan's tie. A soft smile played on her lips, her eyes shimmering with warmth.

"Your tie was crooked."

Ethan suddenly pulled her close, his arm wrapping around her waist. His deep voice brushed against her ear. "Wait for me."

"Mm."

She watched his car disappear down the driveway before turning back to the house. She didn't notice the vehicle accelerating sharply around the corner.

Inside a private room at the Royal Emperor Club, Isabella pressed herself against Colin, her cheeks flushed. Colin stood rigid, beads of sweat forming on his forehead.

"Where's Mr. Sullivan...?"

The door burst open. Ethan's imposing figure appeared in the doorway, and Colin nearly wept with relief.

"Mr. Sullivan!"

Ethan's cold gaze swept over Isabella's dazed state. "The doctor is on the way."

Colin looked miserable, his shirt unbuttoned at the collar.

"The business partners spiked her drink. By the time I realized—"

"Handle it," Ethan cut him off. "Next time, call a doctor immediately."

An hour later, the doctor put away his stethoscope.

"She'll be fine once the drugs wear off."

Ethan turned to leave. Colin hurried after him. "Sir, my phone broke—"

Ethan paused, tossing him a keycard. "Use mine."

After settling Isabella in a room, Colin exhaled in relief. The moment he stepped out of the hotel, Ethan's call came through.

"Find Evelyn."

Meanwhile, Evelyn stood before the largest private room at LoseDemon. She took a deep breath and pushed the door open.

The room fell silent.

A man wearing a demon mask lounged on the sofa, idly tapping his glass.

"Iris, did you like my gift?"

Evelyn met his gaze. "Scorpion, we need to talk."

He chuckled, his eyes glinting coldly behind the mask.

"Talk? You didn't want to talk when you slaughtered twelve of my men."

Her fists clenched. "That was a mission."

"Pity." Scorpion rose slowly. "I don't take missions anymore. Only revenge."

The bodyguards in the room stepped forward in unison. Evelyn narrowed her eyes, her hand subtly moving toward her waist.

"Then only one of us walks out alive tonight."

###Chapter 289

"I could let you go... if you do something for me."

Evelyn Sullivan stepped out of LoseDemon, Scorpion's icy voice still echoing in her ears. Though he claimed to give her time to consider, she knew there was no real choice.

Her mind weighed heavy as she walked toward the parking lot. Just as her fingers brushed the car door, a sharp voice cut through the silence.

"Evelyn!"

She spun around. Ethan Sullivan stood three meters away, impeccably dressed in a suit, his eyes frosty.

"What are you doing here at this hour? You should be home asleep."

Her breath hitched. She hadn't sensed his approach.

"Did you come looking for me?" she asked softly.

He closed the distance in long strides, his shadow engulfing her. "Answer the question."

"It's personal." She turned her face away. "Do I have to explain?"

The air turned glacial.

After a long pause, Ethan turned and yanked open the car door. "Get in."

The ride was suffocatingly silent. Evelyn stared at the neon lights flashing past the window while Ethan's knuckles whitened around the steering wheel.

At the villa, she muttered a quick "goodnight" and retreated to the guest room. Ethan stared at the closed door, his gaze darkening.

They'd started over, yet her secrets only multiplied.

The next morning, Colin Keller placed an investigation report on Ethan's desk.

"Ms. Sullivan entered a VIP room at LoseDemon last night, but all surveillance footage was erased. We can't identify who she met."

Ethan crushed the pen in his hand, ink splattering across the documents.

"Keep digging."

"Sir..." Colin hesitated. "Unless Ms. Sullivan herself tells us—"

The office temperature plummeted. Colin held his breath until Ethan finally growled, "Get out."

Once alone, Ethan dialed an encrypted number.

"I need everything on Scorpion."

Meanwhile, in the MY conference room, Sophia Reynolds nudged Evelyn for the third time.

After the meeting, Sophia cornered her. "Trouble with Ethan?"

"Just tired." Evelyn rubbed her temples.

"Take a break."

"No need." Evelyn hesitated. "About your father..."

"Follow the law." Sophia's voice was firm. "No special treatment."

Silence reclaimed the office. Evelyn stared at her phone, then finally dialed a memorized number.

"Changed your mind?" Scorpion's voice dripped with amusement. "My dear Iris."

###Chapter 290

"I accept your terms from last night."

Scorpion's laughter crackled through the phone, laced with amusement.

"Smart people make smart choices."

Evelyn Sullivan's grip tightened around her phone, her knuckles turning white.

"Remember your promise. If anyone I care about loses so much as a single hair, I'll make you wish you were never born."

"See you in three months."

The call ended, plunging the office into silence. She stared at the darkened screen, exhaling slowly.

——

The penthouse suite of Grand Hyatt.

Isabella Jackson woke with a body that ached as if it had been run over by a truck. Her panicked gaze darted around the room until she confirmed her clothes were intact.

Fragmented memories flashed through her mind—the drink, the dizziness, and... Ethan Sullivan's silhouette?

Her trembling fingers dialed Colin Keller's number.

"Was there something in my drink last night?"

After hearing his explanation, her nails dug into her palms unconsciously.

"Did... Ethan come?"

The unnatural pause on the other end made her pulse quicken.

"You must have imagined it."

Hanging up, Isabella stood before the bathroom mirror with a cold smile. The front desk had confirmed her suspicion—the room was registered under Ethan's name.

"Colin..." She wiped the smudged lipstick from her mouth, her eyes glinting with malice.

——

The Jackson family villa blazed with light.

William Jackson's expression darkened further at the sight of her.

"Why did you hide the MY situation from me?"

Isabella hesitated briefly before donning an innocent look.

"Brocade has been keeping me too busy..."

Of course she wouldn't admit she'd planned to take this secret to her grave.

Grandma Eleanor's call came sooner than expected.

"Evelyn's status has changed now. You must—"

William cut her off impatiently. "I know my limits."

After hanging up, father and daughter exchanged loaded glances. The chandelier's light cast shifting shadows across Isabella's face, revealing the storm brewing in her eyes.

###Chapter 291

"How could she become CEO of MY when she knows nothing?" Victoria Farley's voice dripped with disbelief.

William Jackson pondered for a moment before speaking slowly. "Ethan Sullivan must have given it to her. Weren't the Sullivans acquiring MY recently?"

"He gave Brocade to Isabella, and now MY to Evelyn. What's his game?" Victoria's voice rose sharply. "Does he want both of them?!"

William narrowed his eyes. If Ethan truly intended that, he wouldn't mind offering both daughters. To him, they were merely bargaining chips. Only his illegitimate son, raised in secret, was the true heir to the Jackson fortune.

"I'll find a way to sound Ethan out."

After hanging up, William hesitated before dialing Evelyn's number.

In the conference room, Evelyn was reviewing quarterly reports when her phone screen suddenly projected onto the display—William's caller ID glaringly obvious.

Quincy Howard tensed. "Ms. Sullivan, this—"

"Decline it." Evelyn didn't even glance up. "Continue the presentation."

William listened to the dial tone, his expression darkening. The girl was still holding a grudge. He'd have to visit MY in person. It was a perfect opportunity to assess the company's potential—perhaps a stepping stone for Jackson Group's expansion into fashion.

The vision of his empire growing brought an unconscious smirk to his lips.

"Ms. Sullivan, your father is waiting in the reception room," River Blue said cautiously.

Evelyn paused mid-step, her gaze turning icy. "Turn him away next time."

River realized her mistake and quickly apologized.

Pushing open the reception room door, Evelyn didn't bother sitting. "What do you want, Mr. Jackson?"

William suppressed his anger and forced a smile. "Evelyn, it's been so long since you came home. Join us for dinner tonight. Your mother and sister miss you."

Evelyn nearly laughed out loud. Victoria and Isabella missing her? More like wishing she'd vanish forever.

"Mr. Jackson, we severed ties long ago." She turned to leave. "This had better be your last visit to MY."

"Wait!" William stood abruptly. "Blood is thicker than water. We're still family!"

Evelyn looked back, her eyes mocking. "You're only here because you found out I'm MY's CEO. Suddenly, I'm useful?"

William's face twisted. "Nonsense! I'm your father. Do you really think I'd harm you?"

"You abandoned me twenty-three years ago on a fortune teller's whim. You cut me off for the White family's sake. And let's not forget a lifetime of favoring Isabella." Evelyn enunciated each word. "Whatever you're after, forget it."

Leaving William seething, Evelyn walked away without a backward glance.

Back in her office, Sophia Reynolds lounged with crossed legs, waiting. "Sign this." She leaned in conspiratorially. "Guess who Design just hired?"

###Chapter 292

"Who?" Evelyn Sullivan didn't look up from her desk.

"Fiona Ferguson!" Sophia Reynolds leaned excitedly over the office table.

Evelyn's fountain pen paused mid-stroke. After a moment's thought, she shook her head. "Don't recall."

Sophia's eyes sparkled. "You're right! We'll dominate the industry soon enough!"

Evelyn ended the call and blocked the number without hesitation.

Isabella stared at her phone, then burst into laughter. She turned to her secretary mid-report. "What happened to last quarter's sales figures?"

Lily Lu nervously presented the documents. "Only half of MY's numbers..."

"That timeline might be..."

###Chapter 293

"Isabella, do you have too much free time on your hands?" Evelyn slammed the documents onto the desk. "The design department's progress is unacceptable. What kind of director are you?"

Lily Lu paled. "Evelyn, we've been working overtime—"

Lily clenched her fists, nails digging into her palms.

"Fifty?! Is she insane?"

Evelyn stared at her computer screen, unable to focus.

"There was an urgent matter at the office—"

In the underground parking lot.

"It was an accident. Her client kept pressuring her to drink, and Colin was unavailable—"
